Councilor of Executive Yuan Arrives in Beiping to Investigate War Zone Agricultural Relief 8

(Beiping) Zhang Cao, a councilor of the Executive Yuan, arrived in Beiping to investigate the methods of agricultural relief in the war zone and their difficulties, for reference and research. The agricultural relief work will be completed by the end of April. There are now 2,332 mutual aid societies established and recognized by the group, with 108,847 members and loans of 649,687 yuan. After the agricultural relief is completed, rural cooperative affairs will be handled. (9th Central News Agency)

In the Last Two Weeks, the Number of Chinese Laborers Going to Rehe Has Reached More Than 5,400 9

(Tianjin) According to Gubeikou, in the last two weeks, more than 5,400 Chinese laborers have passed through the pass to Pingquan, Rehe. They are all led by traitors and are closely monitored. Those who cannot bear the arduous journey and try to escape are all caught and brought back. (9th Special Dispatch)

Most Miners in Tangshan Have Resumed Work in the Inner Shift; Worker Groups Request Unconditional Resumption of Work; Mine Bureau Did Not Fully Agree for Safety Reasons; Zhao Dazhong Said to Have Fled to Yuguan; So-Called War Zone General Workers' Union Ceases Activities; Zhao Lei Demands 30,000 Yuan in Travel Expenses for Zhao Dazhong 10

(Tianjin) Asami, the captain of the Japanese garrison in Tangshan, stated that the Japanese side is unwilling to take the blame for others, nor is it willing to be suspected of protecting Zhao Dazhong, but since it concerns the security and order of the war zone, the Japanese side cannot ignore it. Therefore, it is hoped that the Chinese authorities will handle this matter with caution. The Kailuan Mining Bureau received a report this morning that more and more workers in the Tangshan mine's inner shift went down the mine today, with 60-70% implementing the work under the lights. This morning at 6 o'clock, the striking miners gathered outside the mine's office, requesting to be given work and agreeing to return to work unconditionally. The mine manager, fearing that the workers would deceive him and carry out destructive measures after going down the mine, refused. The workers insisted that they had no other intentions and sincerely wanted to resume work. The mine manager then telegraphed for several security teams to guard outside the mine entrance, and selected five or six hundred good people, ordering them to return to work that morning. The others were told to wait until the mine bureau received an official announcement of a solution from the government before they would be allowed to return to work. Thousands of workers who were not allowed to return to work all frowned and hurriedly dispersed. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The first battalion of the first regiment of the war zone security team was ordered by the provincial government on the evening of the 8th to leave its defense area in Luan County and go to Tangshan to assist the Tangshan Public Security Bureau's security team in preventing accidents. Currently, rumors are rife in Tangshan, saying that the garrison team of a certain country is displeased because our side wants to arrest Zhao Dazhong, and will take decisive punitive measures, so the people are becoming increasingly panicked. On the night of the 8th, the Public Security Bureau cooperated with the security team to be on guard all night, and fortunately nothing happened. Today, the streets of Tangshan are plastered with announcements urging workers to quickly repent and return to work, not to be used by Zhao Dazhong, and pointing out evidence that Zhao is a traitor, but without the official names of any organizations. The War Zone Workers' Autonomous United General Union, located on Guangdong Street in Tangshan, is no longer staffed, with only a few servants watching the house. Zhang Zhenfu and Ma Deliang have both gone into hiding and no longer call themselves labor representatives. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) On the evening of the 9th, the Luan-Yu Commissioner's Office issued a notice, setting a deadline of 1 a.m. on the 10th for the Tangshan mine workers on the inner shift and three days for workers on the outer shift to unconditionally return to work. Those who disobey will be dismissed and arrested. Martial law was imposed in Tangshan from noon on the 9th and intensified at night. The security team and police were all mobilized, extensively searching for the leaders of the strike, Zhao Dazhong. At 4:30 p.m. on the 9th, protected by a Japanese named Nakamura, he fled to Shanhaiguan. According to the Commissioner's Office's announcement, all new and old workers' unions in Tangshan are dissolved. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Zhao Lei continues to defend Zhao Dazhong, still demanding 20,000 yuan in travel expenses, even saying that if the authorities or the mine side are stingy, a bloody tragedy will occur. Tao Shangming, Zhao Xunwei, and Zhao Lei invited Zhao on the evening of the 8th to discuss Zhao Dazhong's departure, but no decision was made after several hours. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry believes that the Tangshan mine strike has complex contents. In order to clarify the truth and facilitate handling, it has sent personnel to Tianjin to go and investigate. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Beiping) Zhu Shiqin, on behalf of He Yingqin, went to Tangshan to resolve the Kailuan mine strike and returned to Beiping on the 9th. At 11 a.m., he visited He to report on his mission. It is said that the Kailuan worker unrest has no background, but was incited by the traitor Zhao Dazhong, taking advantage of Tao Shangming's inability to command the security team and public security police. After I arrived in Tangshan, I summoned Zhao Lei and Zhao Xun, and earnestly advised them, and strictly ordered the dispatch of teams to resolve the worker unrest. If they did not obey the order, the security team would be disbanded. Zhao and others then dispatched teams to arrest the traitors, and Zhao Dazhong also fled to Yu, and the worker unrest came to an end. The miners have been given a deadline of the 9th to return to work. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The provincial government telephoned this morning, urging Tao Shangming, the commissioner of the Tangshan Special Administrative District, to quickly resolve the mine unrest. Tao Shangming, because Zhao Lei is protecting Zhao Dazhong, cannot arrest him. This morning, he specifically sent Zhu Zhenwu, the secretary of the commissioner's office, to Tianjin to ask Chairman Yu for instructions on how to handle the matter, and to report on the current situation of the worker unrest. Yu ordered that the original order be followed, and ordered the secretary to return to Tangshan that evening to convey the order. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) According to a Tangshan phone call, in order to obtain 20,000 yuan in travel expenses for Zhao Dazhong, Zhao Lei hosted the Japanese garrison captain Asami and Tao Shangming, Zhao Xun, and others at the Jingzhou Hotel in Tangshan tonight to discuss ways to obtain the money. Zhao Dazhong is still hiding in Tangshan, and has not gone elsewhere. It is rumored that Zhao Lei has sent him to Yuguan, but the authorities have not yet received a report. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) This morning, Zhu Shiqin, the section chief of the Beiping Military Branch, returned to Beiping from Tangshan to report on the truth of the mine unrest. The Tangshan Public Security Bureau arrested Shi Yuzhu, a representative of the troublesome workers who participated in the strike movement, at the Jingzhou Hotel on the night of the 8th, and took him to the Public Security Bureau for questioning. (9th Special Dispatch)

President Wang Changes Schedule to Fly to Jiangxi This Morning; Huang Fu Still Remains in Nanchang 11

(Nanjing) President Wang originally planned to take a Ford plane to Jiangxi on the morning of the 9th, but because the sky was cloudy and the air pressure was too low to fly, he decided to take the Zhongshan ship instead. The ship was ordered to dock at the naval wharf, light its fire, and be ready to depart. The naval band and others also went to the wharf to prepare to see him off. At 7 p.m., Wang notified the naval wharf by telephone, saying that he would not depart for the time being. The band and others then withdrew. It is learned that Wang had a banquet in the evening and could not make the trip. If the weather turns clear on the morning of the 10th, he will still take the Ford plane, otherwise he will take the Zhongshan ship. (9th Special Dispatch)

(Nanchang) Huang Fu did not leave Jiangxi on the 9th, and continued to discuss military and political issues in North China with Chairman Chiang. He will have to stay here for a few more days. (9th Special Dispatch)

Reports on Central and National Government Memorial Weeks; Zhang Ji: Rescuing the Declining Morale; Kong Xiangxi: Stabilizing the Silver Price 13

(Nanjing) The Central Government held its 125th Memorial Week on the morning of the 9th. Ye Chucang, Zhang Ji, Liu Shouzhong, Fang Juehui, Deng Jiayan, Li Zonghuang, Xiao Jishan, Kexing'e, and other staff members, totaling over six hundred people, attended. Ye Chucang presided over the meeting. Zhang Ji reported, stating that at this time when the country is in danger, the people of the whole country are still very depressed and decadent, and the habit of falling and dissipation is becoming more and more serious, which is truly frightening. Therefore, Chairman Chiang's promotion of the New Life Movement is indeed the best way to awaken the people to save the country from danger. I believe that its meaning should be further elaborated, and the power of the party should be used to actively promote it, imitating the methods of Italy and Germany to revitalize the country, to rescue the declining morale, to awaken our national soul through the new life of the people, and to establish a strong nationalism. Only then can saving the country from danger be effective. Dr. Sun Yat-sen also said that the Chinese revolution is inheriting the inherent traditions of Chinese history, so we should not rely on others and lose the inherent morality and spirit of our nation's propriety, righteousness, integrity, and sense of shame. Only by using the inherent spirit of the nation can we awaken the people to strive for rejuvenation. This is also the case in various European and American countries. The government should no longer indulge the people's declining morale, and must be good at guiding and correcting it. I hope that all comrades will strive to promote the New Life Movement. (9th Central News Agency)

(Nanjing) The National Government held its Memorial Week on the morning of the 9th. Deng Jiayan, Chen Gongbo, Tang Shengzhi, Li Yuanding, Chu Minyi, Liu Shouzhong, Kong Xiangxi, Lin Xiang, Chen Qicai, Cao Haosen, Wei Huai, Lu Chao, and staff members from various ministries and commissions, totaling over three hundred people, attended. After Chairman Lin led the ceremony, Kong Xiangxi reported, stating that since the government approved the silver agreement through legislative procedures with reservations, domestic people have been discussing the pros and cons of the silver price and its impact on our country. Some say that China is an importing country and the increase in silver prices will affect the export of national goods in international trade, and foreign goods can be dumped. Some say that our country is in urgent need of revitalizing industry, and the increase in silver prices can allow us to purchase a large amount of machinery with a small amount of silver, which is not without benefit to our country. I, as the head of finance, am not in a position to express my opinion. However, regardless of the silver price, I believe that stabilizing the silver price is the most important thing, so that our country can overcome this difficult situation in the midst of the world economic panic. (9th Central News Agency)

This is not only unprecedented in China in the past, but even foreigners find it difficult to do." Chiang then explained that the recent order that publications should not use foreign characters for year numbers on the cover unless necessary was an order to the political training staff of the Headquarters, but the Political Training Department sent it to the Central Propaganda Committee to be circulated throughout the country, which is absurd. I, Chiang Kai-shek, am not the Central Party Headquarters, not the government. How can my order be given to the Central Propaganda Committee and circulated throughout the country? Isn't that a joke? I hope that all staff members will clearly identify the system and understand the procedures when handling affairs in the future, so that they can share the burden for those above and not mess things up. Commentary: Thoughts on Coping with the North China Crisis 25

— Zhen

In recent days, the situation in North China, according to dispatches from Peiping [Beijing], is gradually revealing a crisis. Firstly, the takeover of the Malanyu area has virtually stalled. Furthermore, over a hundred Japanese reserve officers are traveling to Hebei, Shandong, Chahar, and Suiyuan under the guise of tourism, but their actual intentions are difficult to ascertain. Simultaneously, a large number of Japanese aircraft have arrived in Malanyu, and military exercises are being conducted in the war zone (i.e., the area east of Tianjin and north of Ji County), which is particularly alarming. Moreover, Japanese aircraft are flying over eastern Chahar, spying everywhere, seemingly as a prelude to military action. The puppet troops of Li Shouxin are also stationed within the territory of Guyuan, posing a constant threat of provocation. Thirdly, the labor unrest in Tangshan remains unresolved. While it may appear to be a simple labor-management dispute, the leader of the movement, Li Dazhong, is not a worker and there are also firearms involved, suggesting hidden agendas. These are just a few of the major issues in the complex situation. Investigating the underlying crisis, it's clear that a single incident could trigger a chain reaction, plunging North China into tragedy. As a prominent figure has stated, if there is no comprehensive and concrete strategy to deal with the situation diplomatically, the hidden anxieties about the future will be immeasurable. Diplomacy must be backed by national strength. The central government is focused on strengthening its own power. The saying "internal stability before external resistance" embodies this principle. The current crisis is even more urgent than after the Mukden Incident and before the loss of Rehe. At that time, countries around the world had not yet actively implemented economic nationalism, and relations with Japan were not as strained as they are now. The international community still expressed moral sympathy towards us. As long as we made concrete preparations, there was still room for maneuver. Now, international diplomacy has reverted to the state it was in before 1914, especially in the Far East. How can our country escape danger and achieve national rejuvenation in this difficult situation? Can we afford to delay any longer and not pay close attention?

The key to internal stability lies in the people's livelihood. Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings have clearly articulated this. Today, China's national economy is on the verge of collapse. Even in Shanghai, the market has shown deep panic since the spring, indicating a precarious future for our national economy. Even without external threats, the situation is deeply worrying. Therefore, to achieve genuine internal stability, we must make tenfold the effort to improve the national economy. It is undeniable that our industry is backward, and the decline of rural areas has undermined the foundation of our agricultural nation. To reverse this decline, we must first focus on increasing agricultural production and improving the consumption levels of farmers. The living standards of Chinese farmers have already fallen to the lowest possible level. While eliminating extravagance and promoting frugality are important in urban areas, we should focus on encouraging the improvement of living standards for the common people in rural areas. However, in rural areas today, grain prices are low, side businesses are declining, and economic circulation is on the verge of collapse. In provinces like Henan, Sichuan, Shaanxi, and Gansu, even a small amount of one yuan is considered a treasure. Illegal banknotes flood the market, and the suffering of farmers is hard to describe. Therefore, we should quickly implement credit cooperatives to provide some financial flexibility to the rural economy, and then seek a balance between production and consumption. If the rural economy can truly recover, the construction of new industries will have a clear path forward. The construction of railways, the consumption of textiles, and the promotion of other transportation industries may seem to be within the scope of industrial revitalization, but they are all based on agriculture. In this era of self-sufficiency, the raw materials for our domestic industries must come from our own country. As for national defense preparations, all military facilities and the supply of military necessities depend on the supply of food and raw materials from agriculture. While weapons require a solid industrial foundation, they also rely on a prosperous economy to cope with international changes. Given the urgency of the current international crisis, is it too slow to calmly discuss the economy and military preparations? However, it must be understood that if we cannot overcome the economic difficulties and build a foundation from agriculture and industry, then national defense construction will remain empty words. A gradual approach is ultimately the most fundamental and crucial strategy.

Elections Begin in the United States; Democratic Party Still Able to Maintain Its Advantage 50

(Washington) Tomorrow, the State of Illinois in the United States will hold its primary election. This is the first test of the American people's political views since President Roosevelt defeated the Republican Party in 1932. The political fog is gradually clearing. In this general election, the Democratic Party will still be able to maintain its strength in both the Senate and the House of Representatives. Prominent figures in the Republican Party predict that the party will lose four seats in the Senate in the upcoming general election, while gaining fifty to sixty seats in the House of Representatives. Many Republicans consider this pessimistic, but there is factual evidence for these gains and losses. The Democratic Party currently holds a majority of 191 seats in the House of Representatives. Even if the Democratic Party's power is not as strong as it is today in the upcoming general election, it will certainly not lose all 191 seats. If the Republican Party wants to control the Senate in the upcoming general election, it must not only hold onto its current seats in the Senate but also win fourteen seats currently held by the Democratic Party. As it stands, the Republican Party has no ability to do this. Even if the Republican Party goes all out to face the upcoming parliament and assumes that it can get the vote of Senator Shipstead of the Minnesota Farmer-Labor Party, it can only cause the Democratic Party to lose thirteen seats in the Senate. The total number of seats to be changed in the upcoming general election is 435 in the House of Representatives, 35 in the Senate, and 35 governorships in various states. The primary elections in South Dakota and Alabama will be held on May 1, after Illinois. The primary election in Indiana will be held on May 8, which will also affect the seat of Republican Senator Robinson. Robinson previously loudly opposed the government's austerity policy, advocated for the interests of American veterans in the European War, and ridiculed the American government's failure to obtain repayment of war debts from foreign countries. The states of Pennsylvania, New Jersey, and Connecticut will also hold primary elections in mid-May, while North Carolina, Iowa, California, Florida, Oregon, and Minnesota will hold primary elections in mid-June. The states of Oklahoma, Montana, and Texas will hold primary elections in mid-July. The primary elections in other states will generally be held in mid-August and September. Delaware, New Mexico, Connecticut, Rhode Island, and Utah are exceptions because there are no legal regulations for primary elections in these states. Therefore, the dates of the primary elections in these states are determined by the central committees of each party. The terms of office for the Senate seats of the Democratic Party (17 seats), the Republican Party (17 seats), and the Farmer-Labor Party (1 seat) will expire this year. During the past political wave in the United States, President Roosevelt received great support in both houses of Congress. The number of seats held by each party in the two houses is as follows: (Senate) Democratic Party: 60 seats, Republican Party: 35 seats, Farmer-Labor Party: 1 seat; (House of Representatives) Democratic Party: 313 seats, Republican Party: 113 seats, Farmer-Labor Party: 5 seats. Since the establishment of the Roosevelt administration in 1932, there have been no Republicans in the administrative departments. There are currently nine Republican governors, eight of whom will have their terms expire this year. The other one is Buck, who is currently the Governor of Delaware, and his term will expire in 1937. The Farmer-Labor Party only has one governor, Olson, whose term will also expire this year. (National telegram, 9th)

Hirota's Diplomacy Contains a Conspiracy to Invade China and Russia; Only Willing to Sign a Non-Aggression Pact with the United States; Minister of War Hayashi Holds Prime Minister Saito Hostage 51

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Hirota believes that it is necessary to negotiate a ten-year or even permanent separate non-aggression treaty between Japan and the United States as a preparatory step for the upcoming disarmament conference. However, American officials are highly skeptical of this proposal, wondering whether Japan will refrain from aggressive activities in the Far East after the establishment of a separate Japan-U.S. non-aggression treaty or non-war treaty. Therefore, they informally suggest that the separate Japan-U.S. treaty should be expanded into a multilateral non-aggression treaty involving China, the United States, Russia, and Japan. Hirota responds that while the intention to make it a multilateral treaty is understandable, it is necessary to resolve outstanding issues such as the Sino-Soviet dispute over the Chinese Eastern Railway and the Manchurian issue with China before such a treaty can be considered. He is determined to continue efforts to establish a separate Japan-U.S. treaty based on this view. (Dentsu telegram, 9th)

(Tokyo) Minister of War Hayashi, following the lead of former Minister of War Araki's advocacy for national defense policies, met with Araki on the night of the 2nd to discuss these policies and will meet with him several more times to hear the content and aspirations of his proposed policies. He will then use these as the foundation for carefully drafting his own policies. The core of Hayashi's proposed policies leans toward resolving the Manchurian problem, with a focus on strengthening Japan-Manchukuo cooperation and the economy and industry of Jiangzhou. According to Hayashi, he is still unclear on how to propose these policies to Prime Minister Saito, but he believes that the Manchurian problem is the most important from a national defense perspective. (Dentsu telegram, 9th)

(Tokyo) Minister of War Hayashi plans to visit Prime Minister Saito before the cabinet meeting on the 10th to discuss important policies. He generally believes that the cabinet's mission will end after the parliament adjourns, and that maintaining the status quo may not be advantageous given the objective circumstances. He will convey this intention to Prime Minister Saito, hoping to give the Prime Minister a great impetus. Hayashi also has considerable practical policies for establishing domestic and national policies and for breaking out of the extraordinary situation. There are doubts about whether Prime Minister Saito has the conviction to resolve the remaining disciplinary problems from the parliamentary session. It is said that Hayashi will first report on his visit to Prince Saionji and the proceedings of the cabinet meetings after his departure from Tokyo so as to understand the recent situation and to discuss the above-mentioned issues. In short, the results of the meeting between Hayashi and Saito will have a significant impact on the political situation, and all parties are paying close attention. (Nichi-Rengo telegram, 9th)

The Ministry of Commerce and Industry has recently decided on the following fundamental policies to increase Japanese exports: (1) Adopt a market diversification strategy to reduce the impact of various countries' oppression of Japanese goods; (2) Emphasize small markets in various regions and implement export controls at the same time. Significance of US Fleet Exercise: Said to Be a Friendly Gesture Towards Japan 59

(Washington) The US fleet will depart on April 9, from San Pedro to San Diego, for a transatlantic exercise. Diplomats from various countries here will hold celebrations because this move is actually a friendly gesture towards Japan, sufficient to express the United States' desire to maintain peace in the Pacific. In 1932, the fleet gathered with the battle fleet in San Diego for exercises, appearing on the Pacific Ocean. The fleet also deployed a part of naval aircraft. After the United States recognized Soviet Russia, it formally issued a notice, stating that the fleet would go to the Atlantic for exercises. It was previously rumored that the United States and Russia had discussed the policy of handling the Pacific, conspiring against Japan. The fleet is prepared to return to the Pacific in the autumn, but the US authorities will declare to the world that this exercise will not cause tension in the Pacific. Participating in this exercise are 110 battleships and cruisers, 3,000 officers, and 10,000 soldiers. This large fleet will depart tomorrow, with Admiral Sellers as the commander-in-chief, stationed on the battleship Pennsylvania. The exercise will last until May 31, and will then gather in the Hudson River, at which time President Roosevelt will hold a grand review, and the naval commander-in-chief will also attend. It is learned that the US Navy held a review in December 1918 after the Great War, and President Hoover also held a review in May 1930. This fleet is scheduled to conduct combat exercises when passing through New York on April 19, and will also go to the Panama Canal for an attack, and then return to the aviation base in California. After this exercise, it is heard that Admiral Lefferts will be appointed as the Commander-in-Chief of the US Navy, and Sellers will be appointed as the principal of the Naval Academy. (9th National News Agency)

Japan Demands Britain Abolish Singapore Naval Base; If Britain Ignores It, It Will Overthrow Naval Ratio 60

According to the Tokyo Hochi Shimbun on the 5th, the United States' Far East naval policy has recently adopted an aggressive approach. Initially, due to the expansion plan of the Australian naval base, adding the Australian fleet, the next step is the construction of the Singapore naval base. The naval base is scheduled to be completed before the Third Washington Naval Disarmament Conference, in September 1935. If the port is completed, in maritime strategy, it can control the Indian Ocean and the China Sea, and include the Sea of Japan and the Pacific Ocean. Therefore, its value in terms of both offense and defense is greater than the US Pearl Harbor naval base. (From Sasebo, Japan, to Singapore, it is nearly 900 miles closer than Yokosuka to Pearl Harbor.) It poses a great threat to Japan's national defense, and the balance of national defense power between Japan, Britain, and the United States in the Pacific is disrupted, especially undermining Japan's national defense plan at its root. That is, at the 1935 Washington Conference, Japan's sense of security in national defense was greatly hindered. Therefore, the Japanese authorities directly asked the United States to abolish the facilities of the Singapore naval base. The reasons are: (1) The completion of the Singapore naval base, geographically and technically speaking, causes significant anxiety to both Japan and the United States, resulting in the expansion of Japanese and US armaments, violating the spirit of disarmament. (2) The location of the Singapore naval base, according to the Washington Naval Treaty's Pacific defense restriction agreement area, is only five degrees away from 110 degrees east longitude, then the United States has clearly trampled on the spirit of the disarmament treaty. (3) If it is to protect the East Asian trade route, Hong Kong already has sufficient strength, why build a port in Singapore? Based on these three reasons, the United States is asked to abolish it. If the United States ignores it, it will be proposed that the port be included in the Pacific defense restriction agreement area of the London Treaty and subject to defense restrictions. If it is still impossible to implement Japan's主張, then Japan, threatened by the two ports of Pearl Harbor and Singapore, will overthrow the existing ratio of 5:5:3.

China Eastern Railway Business Report, Severely Affected by Military Attacks 61

Berkley: Ludi, the director of the China Eastern Railway Bureau, has submitted to the Railway Council the railway's business performance in 1933. The railway has suffered greatly due to military incidents, bandit disturbances, the continuing economic panic, the impact of the 1932 flood, and the unhealthy competition from neighboring governments' railways and waterways. The other side has also taken various administrative measures of a non-economic nature, so business has been greatly hampered. Mr. Lu listed the latter in detail, and pointed out that a total of 11 intentional train destructions occurred throughout the year, 38 armed searches of trains, 39 attempts to destroy trains, 19 fires, 197 attacks and robberies of railway personnel, 60 railway personnel killed, 99 railway personnel injured, and 400 people kidnapped. The revenue and expenditure for the past year totaled 35,873,000 gold rubles in revenue and 23,733,000 gold rubles in expenditure. Of these, expenditures directly related to railway operations were only 16,084,000 gold rubles. The cash balance on January 1 of this year was 7,355,000 gold rubles. The report claimed that if the Japanese military authorities could repay half of their debt to the railway, the cash balance on January 1 would reach 19,095,000 gold rubles. In addition to repaying the entire debt of the China Eastern Railway of 4,838,000 gold rubles, the cash balance could still net 14,257,000 gold rubles. Mr. Ludi said in the final paragraph of the report that although the operating environment was extremely difficult, the performance was still excellent. The reason for this was the frugality in expenditure, the improvement of operations, the reduction of costs, the hardship and heroism of the employees' service, and the unusual stability of the China Eastern Railway, which is the main enterprise in the area and closely related to the economic life of the area.

(8th TASS)

(Washington) Congress and the industrial sector are gradually showing signs of unease with the policies of the National Recovery Administration, so the authorities are obviously facing increasing difficulties. The legislative bills it refers to are the Securities Exchange Management Act, the bond bill passed last year to protect investors, and the 30-hour weekly work hour bill for various industries. What is most worrying to some Democrats now is the bill proposed by Frazier and Rhenke, advocating the issuance of Federal Reserve notes with an annual interest rate of 1.5%, in order to regulate rural debt financing. It is not certain what kind of action President Roosevelt will take on the above-mentioned proposals, but there is no doubt that Roosevelt will not give up the plan to grant him great power to conclude tariff agreements. However, it is expected that if the President wants to avoid twists and turns, he will definitely sacrifice other plans. (9th Reuters)

Austrian-Swiss Merger Movement Still in its Infancy 67

Vienna: Austria's neighboring countries are wary of Austria's future, and countries around the world are mostly watching the restoration of the Habsburg monarchy. According to information obtained by the Associated Press, a new movement is now being launched in Austria. This new movement is of paramount importance to Austria's future and has received considerable attention in the political sphere. The significance of the new movement lies in permanently resolving Austria's difficulties. The method used is not to link with Switzerland to form a simple political organization, but to form a federation with Switzerland, so that Austria can be in the same position as Switzerland and enjoy internationally recognized neutrality. Some insist that this new movement is still in its infancy, but if we are not forgetful, we can still recall that six months ago, Austrian Minister for Constitutional Revision, Dr. Schuschnigg, intended to merge Switzerland with the Vorarlberg province. Some consider the current new movement to be a Swiss-Austrian merger movement, and its purpose is only to arouse the attention of the Austrian public. The Associated Press reporter spoke by phone with Governor Nattererb of Bregenz, the capital of Vorarlberg province. Although Nattererb expressed his neutrality, he has confirmed the point that the people of Vorarlberg province tend to support the merger plan, and Nattererb solemnly declared that there is still no organized plan regarding the merger event. Mr. Vorarlberg said, "We are neither left-leaning nor right-leaning. The purpose we have held from beginning to end is to seek Austria's peace. If we cannot complete our ambition to maintain Austria's peace, we may as well discuss the plan for a merger between Austria and Switzerland. However, what Austria is most concerned about is an independent and truly democratic country." When the Associated Press reporter asked Nattererb if his so-called independent and democratic country referred to a political system similar to the Swiss government, Nattererb replied, "Yes," and said that a political system similar to the Swiss government would be most welcomed by the Austrian people. It is thought that the merger of Austria and Switzerland will inevitably affect Austria's constitution, and the recognition of the major powers will also be indispensable. However, supporters of the merger plan firmly believe that the merger of Austria and Switzerland will definitely gain the assistance of Italy, because Italy's desire to maintain Austria's independence is nothing more than to enhance the security of the Iron Curtain border. In addition, France will also be able to treat the merger plan with a friendly attitude and discuss it. The country that opposes the merger plan most vigorously should be Germany, because if Austria and Switzerland merge, it will be tantamount to declaring the death sentence for Germany's ambition to annex Austria. (8th National News Agency)

Liu Weili is hereby relieved of his current position. This order also states: Xu Chengxi, Deputy Commander of the 82nd Division of the Army; Pan Yin'nan, Deputy Commander of the 244th Brigade of the 82nd Division; and Zhang Duyu, Deputy Commander of the 246th Brigade, are to await further assignments. Xu Chengxi, Pan Yin'nan, and Zhang Duyu are all hereby relieved of their current positions. This order.

The Lantern Festival at Ta'er Monastery in Qinghai. The most sacred place in the monastery is the Jiangkang. It enshrines Tsongkhapa, the leader of the Gelug school. Tsongkhapa's disciples are the Panchen Lamas and Dalai Lamas. Many people come to the monastery every year to pay homage. The Lantern Festival is extremely lively. 83

Qinghai Correspondence: Ta'er Monastery in Xining is the birthplace of Tsongkhapa, the founder of Tibetan Buddhism. Every year during the Lantern Festival, Buddhist rituals, scripture readings, and a lantern festival commemorating Tsongkhapa are held. Several days before the main event, monks and laypeople from across the province travel to worship Buddha, creating a vibrant and colorful scene. The current state of the monastery, the history of Tsongkhapa, and the details of this year's scripture readings and lantern festival are described below for the benefit of the nation.

Ta'er Monastery is located in the southern countryside of Xining, only forty li away. Every year, in addition to holding scripture readings and lantern festivals during the Lantern Festival, scripture readings are also held on the sixth day of the sixth lunar month. Although it is a Buddhist gathering, Han and Mongol merchants gather to trade goods several days before the event. The area near the monastery is almost completely filled with people, creating a magnificent spectacle. The architecture of the entire monastery is majestic and magnificent, one of the greatest buildings in Qinghai. There are approximately 3,560 lamas, and their residences are all painted white, surrounding the monastery. The land within a radius of more than 200 li is all managed by the monastery, and the annual income is quite substantial. The rare treasures in the monastery, priceless, are mostly tributes from various places, forming an invisible museum. It is estimated that its real estate alone is worth more than the Boxer Indemnity. Its wealth can be imagined. The most sacred place in the monastery is the Jiangkang, which means the holy mausoleum of Buddhism. The exterior is extremely beautiful, divided into upper and lower levels. The upper level is surrounded by cloth curtains, which are only removed on major commemorative days. Both levels are covered with gold-leaf tiles, and the top level has a beautiful treasure dome made of pure gold, its value incalculable. The portrait and remains of Tsongkhapa, the leader of the Gelug school of Buddhism, are enshrined in the "Jiangkang." Hanging above is a portrait painted by Tsongkhapa himself with his own blood. It is said that when he was preaching in Lhasa, Tibet, because he was separated from his beloved mother, he painted this to give to her as a temporary letter. Tsongkhapa was born in the monastery in the fifteenth year of the Ming Yongle era (i.e., 1417 AD). After his birth, a tree grew on the spot where his mother buried his placenta, and the leaves resembled the shape of the Buddha. People treasured it very much, so Tsongkhapa was also called "Baby Buddha." More than 100 li southeast of the monastery, near the Yellow River, is a monastery called Shachong Temple, where the Baby Buddha cut his hair and practiced devoutly. Shachong Temple is grand in scale, with about a thousand households of monks. It is an important place for trade between the Han and Tibetan people and a center for Buddhist gatherings. Other mountains are steep, and the forests are dense. The mountains resemble lotus platforms, and the forests resemble lotus flowers. Those who travel there are reluctant to leave. After Tsongkhapa practiced in that place, he traveled to various places to study Buddhism at the Saga Monastery in Tashilhunpo in Later Tibet. At that time, monks in various parts of Tibet were given preferential treatment by the court, were corrupt and lewd, unrestrained, did not engage in the proper way, and were superstitious in magic, going deep into wrong paths. Baby Buddha, after becoming alarmed, vowed to reform Buddhism, entered the Great Snow Mountain, and quietly practiced asceticism for more than 20 years. After achieving enlightenment, the Tibetan people greatly believed in him. He established another sect, rejected illusionary arts, forbade marrying wives, and changed to wearing yellow robes. This is the Gelug school of Buddhism, which is different from the old-time devotees who wore red robes. The disciples all understand Mahayana Buddhism, value asceticism, and their learning and conduct are outstanding, surpassing the Red Sect disciples. The Yellow Sect then became popular in Tibet. In the fifteenth year of Ming Chenghua (1479), Baby Buddha passed away. He had two great disciples, one named Panchen Lama and one named Dalai Lama, which translates to "illustrious." It is said that the Dalai Lama is the incarnation of Avalokiteśvara, and the Panchen Lama is the incarnation of Vajrapani. They have already reincarnated in India and are enthroned in Lhasa in Former Tibet and Tashilhunpo in Later Tibet, as the religious leaders of the Yellow Sect. Since Baby Buddha forbade marrying wives, he created a method of succession, saying that although the physical bodies of the Panchen Lama and Dalai Lama die, their spirits still attach to human bodies, and they are never extinguished, appearing in turn as the Khubilhan (meaning incarnation) who controls religious power, etc. This is because the various tribes in northern Mongolia are located in remote areas and cannot personally receive Tsongkhapa. The Jiangkang (commonly known as the Grand Sutra Hall) contains a statue of Tsongkhapa, more than five feet tall, made of pure gold, quite magnificent and solemn. The statue sits on an elaborately constructed treasure seat more than eight feet high. The offerings in front of the statue are all cast in gold and silver. Hundreds of sacred lamps shine brightly before Tsongkhapa, reflecting under his statue, with brilliant light, making people dare not look directly. The wooden plank in front of Tsongkhapa's throne has been rubbed with an inch-deep dent due to the bowing and worship of many believers. It is said that almost every day people come to the monastery from Tibet, Mongolia, Gansu, Rehe, Chahar, and Suiyuan to pay homage. Some even come from thousands of miles away, wearing wooden hand guards and prostrating themselves on the ground to the monastery, showing their sincerity. As for the so-called scripture readings, on the morning of the 28th (fifteenth day of the first lunar month), all the monks in the monastery hold scripture readings, worship dances, and Tibetan music. First, several young monks, wrapped in white cloth, with only their eyes exposed like monkeys, come out to dance. Dozens of monks wear various animal masks, strange costumes, and dance with forks and halberds in their hands, in rhythm with the dance, very much in the style of Western dancing. As for the pilgrims, they must buy a few copper coins worth of butter lamps at the entrance and hold them in their hands, circling several times from left to right, and then return the lamps to their original positions. Some also buy them and light them in front of the Buddha statues. Tens of thousands of people crowd together, extremely tense. The monastery has black-robed lamas who act as temporary police, wielding whips to maintain order. The Lantern Festival that evening is dedicated to commemorating Tsongkhapa, made of countless patterns of butter lamps. The ingenious lamp stands are extremely beautiful and exquisite. The first layer is a panorama of Lhasa in Former Tibet. Below it is a large Buddha statue with hands extended, sitting in meditation, kind and gentle. Other Buddha statues, flowers, landscapes, figures, etc., lifelike, and full of emotion, are arranged around, shining like a painting. The artistic genius of Tibet and the boundlessness of Buddhism inspire awe in visitors. When performing the sacrificial rites of the Lantern Festival, a group of black-robed lamas leads the way, followed by a large group of lamas carrying Tibetan incense and sacrificial objects. Behind them is a lama holding a jade scepter, with two lamas on either side each holding a torch. Behind them is carried the incarnation of Tsongkhapa. The crowd walks to the butter lamp stand and the large Buddha statue, kneeling solemnly and respectfully. After the ceremony is completed, the butter lamps also begin to melt at this time. Tens of thousands of people watch the scene, and the grand ceremony is thus concluded.

Changes in European Diplomacy. Germany Faces Difficulties. Italy's External Expansion. Unemployment Numbers Slightly Reduced. Cash Reserves Shaken. 91

German Correspondence

The meeting of the three dictatorial prime ministers, Mussolini of Italy, Dollfuss of Austria, and Gömbös of Hungary, in Rome is a shock to all of Europe. Because Austria and Hungary, under the so-called treaties of Saint-Germain and Trianon, are dominated by the great powers. Whether in politics or in economics, they seem to have no way out, and can even be said to be unable to find a way out. Originally, Austria's situation and ethnic relations made merging with Germany the most suitable. First, because the National Socialist Party acted too recklessly, it lost the hearts of most Austrians. Second, Italy feared that after the Austro-German merger, the German population would jump from 65 million to 72 million, posing a great threat to Italy. Moreover, German science and technology are no match for them. Not only Italy is wary of this, but France is also very cautious and vigilant. Indeed, if Germany and Austria were to merge, France would use various peace treaties as weapons to oppose it, and would also try to undermine any attempt to win over Austria and Hungary. However, they are in agreement on restricting Germany's development, so they tacitly acknowledge the actions of Italy, Austria, and Hungary without immediately taking active measures to contain them. Germany, at this time, if it does not receive solid political assistance, will not act rashly.

Moreover, in terms of economics, it also has internal weaknesses. For example, the unemployment problem. Since the National Socialist Party came to power in January last year, improving the unemployment situation has been its main claim. Since then, according to surveys by labor exchanges, the number of unemployed workers at the end of February last year was more than 6,014,000, and thereafter gradually decreased. However, that kind of decrease contains a very strong seasonal relationship. Because in the summer, after the rise of summer resorts and other temporary businesses, many workers will always be attracted to work. By December of last year, it had increased again. Has Germany's unemployment situation improved after all? According to the report of the German Institute for Economic Research, there were 1.5 million unregistered unemployed workers from the spring to autumn of 1931, and now there are 2 million unregistered unemployed workers. The number of unemployed workers in the winter of last year decreased by more than 1,640,000 compared with the winter of the previous year, while the number of newly employed people increased by only 1,321,000 during the same period. Now, regarding the employment situation of German workers and the unemployment situation, according to the statistics of the German Institute for Economic Research, the table is copied below:

Table of the Number of Unemployed Workers and Employed Workers in Germany (in thousands of people)

November 1933 November 1932

Number of Employed People 14,020 12,699

Number of Registered Unemployed People 3,715 5,355

At least 500,000 to 600,000 unregistered unemployed workers must be added here. What kind of results can the German government achieve with its desperate efforts? Or, after spring goes and summer comes, will there be a seasonal turn for the better as usual?

Furthermore, Germany's international income and expenditure has no overseas investment, and even the income from shipping is very limited, almost negligible. Therefore, it can only rely on trade exports exceeding imports to compensate. However, since the beginning of this year, foreign trade in January and February has suddenly turned to import surpluses. Compared with February of last year, imports increased from 71.5 million marks to 75.9 million marks, while exports decreased from 76.4 million marks to 69.3 million marks. That is, a surplus of 4.9 million marks in exports has turned into a surplus of 6.6 million marks in imports. What a dangerous thing this is. To this end, the German government decided in mid-February to manage foreign exchange, requiring that the purchase of imported goods should not exceed 50% of exports. In March, it was decided to be 45%. Moreover, the cash reserve for convertible notes of the German Reichsbank is only 26.2 million marks, with a reserve ratio of only 8% for 330 million convertible notes. Germany's current economic crisis is no less than its diplomatic plight. (March 9, 1934, in Berlin)

Sun's Troops Near Completion of Reorganization. Men Bingyue Returns to Beiping to Report to He. Sui Army Encircles and Suppresses Yang Hou's Small Bandit Unit. 92

Beiping Correspondence: The reorganization of Sun Dianying's troops is, in general, nearing completion. Men Bingyue, who previously traveled with Fu Zuoyi from Beiping as a representative of the Military Affairs Commission to coordinate all military matters, because the war has ended, needs to return to Beiping to report to He Yingqin regarding the disbandment of Sun's troops and all the events that occurred during the campaign. Therefore, on the 6th, he took the express train on the Ping-Sui Railway and returned to Beiping. After getting off the train, he immediately reported to He. According to Men, the situation of Sun's troops is roughly as follows: "The disarmament, carried out by the Jin-Sui army, has now been fully completed. A total of 12,300 rifles have been obtained, and the number of officers and soldiers has reached 28,000. They are all being housed by the Jin-Sui army in camps set up in the San Shenggong area, and transported to Baotou in batches, and then transported to Hebei. This unit is still commanded by Sun's original regimental commanders Yu Shiming, Liu Yueting, Lu Fengnian, etc. Yu's unit has already advanced towards Linhe. Yu personally arrived in Linhe on the 2nd to meet Commander-in-Chief Fu and ask for instructions on everything. Lu Fengnian and Liu Yueting will also go to Lin to meet Fu and ask for instructions. Sun's troops suffered heavy losses in this operation, especially Liu Yueting's. Liu's unit will be stationed in Dengkou in the future, while Yu and Lu's units will enter Hebei. Those near Ningxia, such as Ding Futing, Yang Ganqing, and Xia Weili, total two brigades. Except for a small part waiting to be reorganized in the suburbs of Ningxia, the majority are still coming north to merge with Yu and Liu. Xia Weili's unit will arrive soon. Sun's troops have been in a state of supply difficulties for more than three months. Their embarrassed state is unprecedented. After disarming, the Jin-Sui army treated them extremely well, so they all felt like they had gone from hell to heaven. Yang Hou, a bandit accumulated in western Sui, knows that the authorities will never tolerate him, so when Sun's army failed, he detoured around western He and fled eastward along the Yin Mountains. He has now fled to the territory of Wuchuan County. That area is slightly north, that is, the League Banner area, which is very close to the provincial capital. The Suiyuan army has already encircled from all sides. The bandits have nearly 2,000 rifles. The Jin-Sui army is very experienced in suppressing bandits, so it should be easy to eliminate this bandit." Tao Jun, Wang Zhongquan, Zhang Xuanze, etc., who were sent by the Military Affairs Commission to monitor the reorganization of Sun's troops, are in the gathering places of Sun's troops, assisting the Jin-Sui army in handling everything. Relay stations have been set up along the way to provide for Sun's troops. "Whether I still need to return west must await the decision of Chairman He," he said. The Suiyuan Provincial Party Department, with spring plowing imminent, has telegraphed to the central government and the Military Affairs Commission requesting the prompt return of the 410,000 yuan that the people of the counties of Wuyuan, Linhe, Baotou, Anbei, etc., in western Sui not only had all their private savings taken away by Sun's army, but also advanced in cash to purchase military supplies for Sun, because if the government does not return the money immediately, it will be difficult for the people of those counties to survive, so they hope that spring plowing can be expected. (7th)

Jiangyin: Bandits Attempt to Rob a Ship, Open Fire and Resist Arrest, Injuring People 93

On the 7th, the Wuxi ship, owned by Hua Kai of the ninth district, arrived at Lujiaqiao at around 7 PM. Suddenly, four bandits disguised as passengers were discovered by the shipowner, Lin Senquan, who secretly reported it to the local defense corps. Instructor Xu Sheng was dispatched with corps members to inspect. Unexpectedly, the bandits opened fire to resist arrest. The bullets struck corps member Wang Genyuan in the face, causing his teeth to fall out, and injured passenger Wang Hongbao in the shoulder and local resident Hou Sanbao in the abdomen, killing him instantly. The injured were sent to Shuzi Hospital for treatment. Seeing they were outnumbered, the bandits fled into the water. Corps members bravely chased them for about a mile, and bandit Zhao Dabao was shot in the leg and captured. Two other bandits, Duan Xiaoquan and Jiang Weixin (both from Tongshan County), were also arrested and taken to the corps headquarters. They confessed to plotting to rob the ship without denying it. Today (the 8th), they were handed over to the county for legal proceedings.

Zhenjiang: Forging Official Documents, Seven-Year Sentence 94

Zhang Xiting, a resident of Xiaomatou, using the alias Liu Lansen, colluded with Li Peigen of Liu Li Lane, using the alias Liu Rentao, and Chen Yeru, along with the fugitive Wu Shaoquan, forged court documents under the pretense of investigating opium cases, defrauding wealthy opium addicts in both urban and rural areas, and not just once. Later, they attempted to defraud Zhao Jinjiang, the manager of Hengkang Pawnshop in Gaozi Town, but were exposed by the victim, who telegraphed the local court to inquire about the alleged investigation of opium cases. He received a reply instructing the arrest of Zhang Xiting and others impersonating court police and their transfer to the court. After multiple interrogations, it was learned that prosecutor Li Weishen had concluded the investigation and indicted the defendants for forging official documents. Judge Gu of the criminal court presided over the trial and sentenced Zhang Xiting and the other two to seven years of imprisonment.

Hangzhou: Two Fires in One Day 95

A flat house at No. 56 Lilong Shezui, Hangzhou, jointly inhabited by Shen Baokun, Chen Yaoqi, and Chen Tingwen, caught fire suddenly at 1:50 PM today (the 9th) due to carelessness while cooking lunch. The fire brigade rushed to the scene upon receiving the alarm and extinguished the blaze after an hour and a half. Four houses, Nos. 57, 59, and 60, were burned down, with losses estimated at around 1,000 yuan. Additionally, Yuanrun Sauce Garden at No. 132 Fansiqian caught fire at 0:20 AM on the 9th due to an electrical short circuit, which spread to three houses, including Zhang Shunxing firewood shop, with losses exceeding 2,000 yuan.

Jiaxing: Shooting Policemen Sent to Court for Investigation 96

Following a conflict between police and civilians on the evening of March 4th, in which a police officer opened fire, killing merchant Shen Jinguang and injuring several others, the local branch court initiated an investigation. It ordered the county magistrate and public security bureau to hand over the police officer who opened fire by a specific date for interrogation. It is now learned that the county public security bureau has sent five police officers – Sun Changgen, Shu Yunfei, Chen Dequan, Zhang Zida, and Yu Zhentang – to the prosecutor's office for interrogation yesterday afternoon. They were released on bail by the team leader Chen Weiping, squad leaders Chen Guoding, police chiefs Jin Derun, Zhao Yuxiang, and Shen Keming.

Tournament Causes Homicide 97

At Taiping Bridge in Jiaxing, a welcoming ceremony was held on the 7th. Unexpectedly, a fight broke out between two sides at Miaoxia Bridge, about four miles away from Taiping Bridge. Gao Zhengxiang (age 28), who lived in Gaojiabang, was severely injured. He was immediately sent to the Gospel Hospital for treatment. He died at 8 AM due to severe injuries. The county public security bureau has ordered the town leader, Mo Huiju, to send the perpetrators, Mo A'nan and Mo Xiaoshang, to the bureau for detention, preparing them for court trial.

Haimen: Wang Shucun Disaster Victims Appeal for Relief 98

Wangyang Village in the tenth district is still in the reclamation and freshwater storage stage. The villagers rely solely on the annual cotton harvest for their livelihood. Last autumn's tidal disaster completely submerged the cotton fields, resulting in no income at all, and the disaster situation is severe. Although the county relief association has provided relief once, it is like a drop in the bucket, insufficient to solve the problem. Currently, during the spring famine, there is a shortage of food. The disaster victims are subsisting on green grass and chaff every day, which is extremely miserable. Yesterday, they specifically sent representatives to the relief association to appeal for immediate relief.

A Homicide During Qingming Tomb Sweeping 99

Shen Goulang, from Shen Goulang, about three miles southeast of Dahong Town in the fifth district, is a butcher. His nephew, Jiaqi, serves in the district's defense team. The uncle and nephew have long had disputes. The day before yesterday (the 5th), during Qingming tomb sweeping, Jiaqi argued with Goulang over the poor quality of the sacrificial offerings, which led to a physical fight. Jiaqi drew his pistol and fired three shots at Goulang, all hitting his head. He fell to the ground and died instantly. Seeing that his goal had been achieved, Jiaqi left without interference. People saw him holding a weapon, and no one dared to stop him. Yesterday (the 6th), the widow filed a petition to the district committee, which was forwarded to the county for inspection, verification of the crime scene, and investigation of the murderer.

Xiaoshan: Failure to Repay Debt Leads to Assault 100

Gu Asong, a resident of Gujiaxi in the southern countryside of Xiaoshan, borrowed one dollar from Ding Guisheng, a villager from Fangjiatang in a neighboring village, last winter, promising to repay it during Qingming Festival. On the 5th, Ding asked Gu for repayment. Instead, Gu gathered over ten people, including A'kun, and hid sharp knives. They rushed to the Ding family's house and stabbed Ding Maomao, Ding Guisheng, Ding Baoting, and Ding Chen's head, back, feet, legs. Then, they rushed to the Chenghuangshan paper factory and destroyed it completely. Ding Guisheng was also stabbed. Villagers reported this illegal activity and took the three seriously injured people to the county for medical examination and requested an investigation.

Local News 101

American Aviator Hawks Flies the Condor Over the City Yesterday Inviting Chinese and Western Guests to Ride; Flies to Hangzhou This Morning, Stays for a Week and Returns to Shanghai 102

American aviator Major Hawks, accompanied by pilot Gore, brought the Condor, a giant military-commercial dual-use aircraft, to China for demonstrations. After arriving in Shanghai, the aircraft parts were transported to Hangzhou for assembly. The entire assembly was completed a few days ago. After several successful test flights in Hangzhou, he flew the aircraft to Shanghai on the 7th. Yesterday afternoon at 2:30 PM, he conducted a test flight at Longhua Airport and invited Chinese and Western guests to ride on a flight around the city. The details are recorded below:

A Glimpse of the Fuselage 103

The Condor aircraft is painted entirely in tile gray, with the Kuomintang emblem of a white sun on a blue sky painted on the underside of both wings. The aircraft is equipped with a 700-horsepower engine on each side. The aircraft's nose and fuselage are surrounded by circular windows for observation. There is a small door on the left side of the fuselage for passengers to enter and exit. There are two pilot seats in the front of the nose. The center seats on both sides can accommodate 24 to 30 passengers, making the fuselage quite large.

Flying Around the City 104

At 2:30 PM, about a hundred Chinese and Western reporters and American men and women arrived at Longhua Airport. They were greeted and boarded by Pan Lai, the Chinese manager of Curtiss-Wright Aircraft Factory. Due to the large number of people, the flights were divided into four trips. Each time, Major Hawks accompanied by pilot Gore flew around the city and Pudong, taking about 30 minutes before safely landing. Although the aircraft's fuselage is large, it flies very stably in the air. Reporters sitting inside did not experience any bumps. Therefore, all the Chinese and Western guests who rode the aircraft yesterday praised the aircraft for its meticulous and great equipment. The guests finally dispersed at 4:15 PM.

Flying to Hangzhou Today 105

According to Pan Lai, the Chinese manager of Curtiss-Wright Aircraft Factory, Major Hawks plans to fly the Condor from Shanghai to Hangzhou this morning with Pan Lai and pilot Gore. He plans to stay in Hangzhou for a week and then return to Shanghai before flying to Nanjing, Hankou, Nanchang, Beiping and other places, and visit Chairman Chiang and Vice Commander Zhang and other authorities.

Aircraft Features 106

Although the aircraft is a commercial aircraft, it can be quickly converted into a military aircraft in times of emergency. It can carry 2,400 pounds of bombs, and the fuselage can hold two large 1,100-pound bombs. All equipment in the aircraft, such as photography and testing equipment, is complete. The fuselage can be equipped with five machine guns and can store 728 gallons of oil. The aircraft's total capacity can carry 17,500 pounds. The speed per hour is 175 miles, so it can fly up to 1,200 miles in one go without landing midway.

After the Establishment of the Flying Club Chairman Chiang's Approval Arrives; Inaugural Meeting of Promoters to Be Convened 107

The Chinese Aviation Association, in order to popularize civilian aviation and encourage the public's interest in flying, specially invited well-known figures in the aviation industry at home and abroad to jointly initiate the organization of a flying club as a place for people to study and learn flying skills. A few months ago, the association drafted a plan outline and Secretary-General Lin Wojiang made a special trip to Beijing to present it to various central agencies for approval. The preparatory office of the association was also established on the 18th of last month during the naming ceremony of the Tianchu aircraft to make active preparations so that it can be completed as soon as possible. Recently, Lin Wojiang went to Hangzhou again to contact the Aviation Department and get military approval.

Special Instructor 108

After Lin returned to Shanghai, a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited him yesterday morning. According to him, the association received a reply from Chairman Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission yesterday, roughly saying that our country has repeatedly suffered painful lessons and deeply feels the urgency of aviation needs. It is appropriate to approve the establishment of the association's ability to understand this purpose and advocate for the public, and to express encouragement and commendation. After receiving this reply, the association immediately sent letters to all promoters to schedule an inaugural meeting to jointly discuss the steps and work policies to be taken. Therefore, the Flying Club can be formally established in a very short period of time.

Foreign News: A Brief Biography of General von Seeckt 109

According to Lin Bao, General von Seeckt, the leader of the German Army during the European War and the man in charge of reorganizing the German Army after the armistice, arrived in Shanghai yesterday aboard the P&O liner Naldera for his second visit to China. His wife also accompanied him. The purpose of this trip has not been revealed. It is currently believed that he will enter Beijing in the coming days to hold talks with the Chinese authorities. The general first came to China last spring, when he served as a consultant to the Chinese government on the reorganization of the army, but this plan was never implemented. The general is now sixty-six years old, comes from a military family, and served as a lieutenant colonel in the army at the beginning of the European War before being promoted to chief of staff of the army commanded by General Mackensen. He then served as chief of staff of the Turkish Army in the war zone. General Mackensen's army intercepted the Russian army's line of defense in the Gorlice area, thus capturing major cities such as Warsaw. This was the result of the general's strategy. He then served in Siberia and Russia as chief of staff of the army commanded by Archduke Charles, suppressing the offensive of General Brusilov. After the armistice in 1918, he participated in the peace negotiations and was then ordered to reorganize the German Army on a non-political basis. This was a difficult task, and the new German military system was created by him. The general then served as commander-in-chief of the German Army until 1926, when he retired. The general wrote a book about his experiences at the peace conference called "Thoughts of a Soldier," which was translated into English several years ago. In the book, he warned that inequality in military strength would cause various harms and could easily lead to war. The general is fond of traveling and has traveled throughout Europe and to several countries in the East. He is particularly interested in India and spent many days there on this trip before boarding the Columbus-class Naldera to China.

The Ruling on the Collision Between the Wanshang and Luan Ships: The Wanshang Was Not at Fault; The Luan Was Responsible 110

On December 12th of last year, the Sanbei Company's Wanshang ship was sailing upstream to Wuhan. It was at night when it reached the vicinity of Fishing Island in Qizhou, upstream of Jiujiang. As the Wanshang was sailing upstream, the Bao Yuan Company's Luan ship, managed by the Jianghan ship of the Wuhan Recruitment Committee and carrying 220 new recruits, was traveling in the opposite direction to Xun. Each ship sounded horns, but collision was inevitable and the Luan ship was hit and immediately sank. All 220 new recruits fell into the water. The Wanshang immediately stopped to help rescue and carried them back to Hankou. As a result, 78 soldiers died. The Wanshang was detained in Hankou for one day and released the next day. The captain of the Wanshang was Weng Ziqing, who was temporarily assigned to the shift by the Qingpu shipowner. Cao Renyu and Yan Weijin were on duty as second officers when the accident occurred, and Xiao Yanqing was on duty as the officer on the Luan ship. An investigation was conducted.

Because the case was of great importance, the Wuhan military authorities, together with the Hankou Navigation Administration Bureau and the owners of the Sanbei and Bao Yuan ships, hired experts in the navigation industry to conduct an arbitration. Before the arbitration, seven impartial personnel recommended by each party went to the Fishing Island area to conduct an on-site investigation and collect testimonies and physical evidence. From mid-January to early February, each impartial person spent half a month investigating to clarify the situation. In mid-February, an arbitration tribunal was established to summon the crew members on duty from both ships and witnesses to take statements as the basis for determining the right and wrong of the case.

Setting up an Arbitration Tribunal 111

The arbitration tribunal was set up in the Hankou Navigation Administration Bureau. The arbitration committee consisted of Zhang Xiunan, Director of the Hankou Navigation Administration Bureau, the head of the Third Section of the bureau, the head of the examination section, the executive committee of the Hankou Shipping Association, and representatives of the Insurance Association. There were also Captain Huang Yushi of the China Merchants Bureau's Jianguo ship and Captain Zheng Dingxi of the Sanbei Changxing ship. From February 15th, Weng Ziqing, Cao Renyu, Yan Weijin, Xiao Yanqing, etc. were summoned to inquire about the sailing conditions of the two ships at the time, the navigation regulations, and the circumstances of the collision. The investigation continued on the 16th, 17th, 18th, and 21st, and witnesses Zhu Kaolan and Fang Zhiping were also summoned. The Customs Commissioner of the Jianghai Customs was also invited to court to present his opinions. The Ministry of the Navy and the Ministry of Communications both attached great importance to this case and sent a representative each to participate in the public trial. The Ministry of Communications appointed Shen Jiyun, the chief shipowner of the China Merchants Bureau, as the chief judge of the committee.

Arbitration Decision 112

After a long period of investigation and interrogation, each arbitrator compiled their opinions and submitted them to Shen Jiyun, who drafted the judgment of the case. It has now been completed, running to tens of thousands of words, detailing the navigation process of the case and attaching legal theories, which is very detailed. The main text states that the Sanbei Wanshang ship collided with the Bao Yuan Company's Luan ship at Fishing Island on December 12th, resulting in the drowning of 78 soldiers, and the responsibility for this incident rests with the Bao An Company's Luan ship.

Eight Reasons 113

The judgment elaborates on the reasons why the Luan ship should be held responsible for this tragedy, totaling eight reasons. The original text is very long, but briefly, when the Luan ship met the Wanshang ship, the red and green lights of the Luan ship appeared alternately. The Wanshang first sounded its whistle once, and the Luan ship responded with two sounds. When it wanted to give way, the Wanshang had already reached the left side of the Fishing Island lighthouse and could no longer give way. It immediately slowed down. The Luan ship showed its green light and sounded its whistle twice, indicating that it was giving way to the right. The Wanshang was deep in the water and had no place to give way, so it sounded its whistle twice and ordered a full port rudder, giving way to the left. Unexpectedly, the bow moved to the left, and the Luan ship suddenly showed its red light. The Wanshang quickly went into full reverse, but in less than a minute, the two ships collided, and the Luan ship immediately sank. This is the first. The Luan ship's crew had poor piloting skills, the rudder was not flexible, and there was no compass on board for long-distance night navigation. Other technical details about navigation are omitted.

Announcement in Hankou 114

This judgment has been stamped with the names of each arbitrator and signed, and has been handed over to Huang Yushi, who is in charge of the case, to be taken to Hankou. It will be announced in both Shanghai and Hankou today, and this tragedy will be resolved. Since the Luan ship sank, all losses should be borne by its shipowner, Bao Yuan Company, and the Sanbei Company is not involved.

Aviation Association: Hotel Industry Conference Held Yesterday to Discuss Ways to Collect Donations for Aviation to Save the Country; It Was Resolved to Start Collecting From the 15th of This Month 122

The Shanghai China Aviation Association convened a meeting of the hotel industry at 4 PM yesterday at the 9th floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge Youth Association to discuss ways to collect donations for aviation to save the country. The details are listed below:

Chairman's Report 123

After the representatives successively took their seats, the chairman first reported (1) the purpose of convening the hotel industry to discuss (2) the process of the Aviation Association raising donations to purchase aircraft. After the report, Lin Wojiang reported and the Shanghai Hotel Industry Collection of Aviation Savings Donations was passed.

Attending Representatives 124

Those who attended yesterday included Wu Tiecheng, captain of the China Aviation Association (represented by Li Dachao), Secretary-General Lin Wojiang, Sun Qiuping, chairman of the Hotel Industry Association, Wu Ruisheng of the Nanjing Hotel, Li Wencai of the Central South Hotel, Zhang Qiyuan of the Great China Hotel, Guan Jichuan of the New Asia Hotel, Tu Guiqing of Yipinxing, Huang Zhijian of Yangtze, Liu Qirun of Jielu, Chen Guoyuan of New World, and representatives from Great Shanghai, Wu Palace, Asia, Mengyuan, Huizhong, Dahu, Yingbin, Yuelai, Santai, and more than 400 others. Chairman Li Dachao resolved the various cases.

Resolved Cases 125

(1) To collect aviation savings donations, 5% will be collected according to the actual price of the room. (2) Collection will begin on April 15th, and the Aviation Association will notify all hotels in the city to collect donations uniformly in conjunction with the municipal government. (3) The collection period was originally set for six months, but if the collection is insufficient at the end of the period, the collection period may be extended. (4) The name of the aircraft purchased by the hotel industry will be designated as the Hotel Industry Aircraft.

Methods Passed 126

Shanghai Hotel Industry Collection of Aviation Savings Donations: (1) The China Aviation Association has formulated these methods in order to raise aviation savings funds. (2) Each hotel will collect an additional 5% of the room rate as an aviation savings donation. (3) Each hotel will collect the aviation savings donations once a week and submit them to the China Aviation Association. (4) Each hotel must issue a receipt for the aviation savings donation and give it to the guest. (5) Each hotel must post the aviation savings donation methods in each room for guests to read. (6) The hotel industry will collect aviation savings donations for a period of six months. (7) The China Aviation Association will print a three-part receipt for the hotel industry aviation savings donations and distribute them to each hotel. (8) The China Aviation Association may send personnel to inspect the donation situation. If there are any malpractices, they shall be punished according to law. (9) The China Aviation Association shall announce the amount of aviation savings donations received from the hotel industry every month. (10) These methods shall be submitted to the government for approval and implementation.

Record of the First Anniversary Commemoration of Mr. Liang Shiyi's Death; Concurrently Holding the Liang Shiyi Academic Award Committee 132

The first anniversary commemoration of Mr. Liang Shiyi's death was held at the Bankers' Association at 5 PM yesterday. Many people from all walks of life attended. In the area of transportation, there were Ye Gongchuo, Zheng Hongnian, Zhong Wenyao, etc. In the area of banking, there were Hu Mengjia, Lu Xuepu, Feng Gengguang, Wu Dingchang, etc. In the area of industry, there were Lin Kanghou, Lin Zhenyao, Chen Huanzhi, etc. In the area of education, there were Dong Renjian, Liao Maoru, Lu Dingkui, etc. Ye Gongchuo was publicly elected as the chief priest, and Liang's sons, Ding Shu and Ding Min, expressed their gratitude. Afterwards, Zheng Hongnian gave a speech, stating that Liang had participated in the revolution and expressed his belief to Empress Dowager Longyu about the surrender of the country. In addition, he described Liang's opposition to Hongxian's claim to the throne at that time. Subsequently, Lu Xuepu gave a speech, describing Liang's creation and management of the Three-Four Year Public Bonds and the establishment of the Stock Exchange. Finally, Ye Gongchuo gave a speech, describing Liang's achievements in managing transportation affairs, especially the recovery of rights and the development of the national economy, which are still regarded as the guiding principles for transportation managers. The former is exemplified by the recovery of the sovereignty of the Shanghai-Nanjing (Beijing-Shanghai) Road General Administration and the redemption of the entire Beijing-Hankou (Pinghan) Road. The latter is exemplified by the transportation of Mongolian tea to Russia via the Pinghan Road. The difficulties in dealing with these matters were often unknown to the Chinese people. He recalled that after the redemption of the Beijing-Hankou Railway, the Qing court only replied with the three words "I know." Thinking about it now, it is truly regrettable. Liang did not care about praise or criticism in his life, and this is one aspect of it. After the meeting, the Academic Award Committee continued to meet to plan which schools and departments should be awarded scholarships for this year's examinations.

The Ministry of Railways is Borrowing 35 Million from Shanghai Banking Circles to Complete the Longhai and Yuehan Railways; It is in Consultation with the Boxer Indemnity Fund to Determine the Issuance of Public Bonds 136

According to Xinsheng News Agency, the Ministry of Railways has borrowed 40 million pounds sterling from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Directors to complete the Longhai and Yuehan Railways. After repeated meetings and investigations by the association, it has long been decided to divide the funds into cash, the material funds of the London Purchasing Committee (that is, using railway materials in lieu of cash), and a portion of public bonds, totaling 40 million pounds sterling. A contract has been signed in Beijing. It is now known that the portion of the loan for issuing public bonds, with an amount of 1.6 million pounds sterling, is being mortgaged by the Ministry of Railways to several large Chinese and foreign banks in Shanghai, such as the China Central Transportation and HSBC, for 1.5 million pounds sterling, which is approximately 35 million yuan in national currency. It is expected that this will soon become a reality.

A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited Mr. Caseleigh, a foreigner involved in this matter, yesterday morning. Mr. Caseleigh admitted the matter and said that the amount of the loan was 1.5 million pounds sterling, but it is still under negotiation and has not been formally decided. It will probably have to go through considerable consultation. As for the interest rate and repayment methods, etc., because it has not been completely decided, the details are still unknown after many inquiries.
