Far East Games Standing Committee Continues Informal Meeting Japan Actually Proposes Performance by Puppet Organization Chinese Representatives Cao and Shen Refute with Reason No Need for Further Discussions at Cathay Hotel This Morning Public Sentiment Has Not Died, Should be Firmly Resisted

The long-awaited Standing Committee meeting of the three countries (China, Japan, and the Philippines) for this year's Far Eastern Games was held yesterday at the office of the Shanghai Football Field on Jiaozhou Road. From 10:00 AM to 12:00 PM, the five agenda items were discussed and completed. In the afternoon, at 2:30 PM, an informal meeting continued, and the Japanese representative actually proposed the issue of a puppet organization participating in a performance. Our representatives immediately and vehemently refuted this. The Japanese representative then directly suggested to the chairman, Dr. Tambuatting of the Philippines, that before discussing this issue, the representatives of each country should be given ample time for consideration, and requested that the meeting be postponed until 9:15 AM tomorrow morning (i.e., this morning) at the Cathay Hotel. The chairman agreed. Thus, the issue of this puppet organization's participation, which is being watched by all, has been formally raised in the three-nation Standing Committee meeting, and our side will participate in the discussion this morning. The details are as follows:

Representatives of the Three Countries Attend the Meeting

Yesterday at 10:00 AM, representatives of the three countries arrived one after another and convened the Standing Committee meeting at the office of the Shanghai Football Field. The attendees included Dr. Tambuatting from the Philippines, Yamamoto and Matsuzawa from Japan, and Gan Seimo, the Japanese Consul in Shanghai. The Chinese representatives were Cao Yunxiang (representing Vice President Wang Zhengting of the General Assembly) and Shen Siliang, a key member of the Sports Advancement Association. At that time, reporters from both Chinese and Japanese newspapers flocked to gather news, and the situation was quite serious.

Cao's Remarks During Break

After the meeting began, Dr. Tambuatting of the Philippines served as chairman, and Zhou Jiaqi recorded the minutes. After the representatives took their seats, Chinese and Japanese photographers released flashbulbs in the room before moving outside. Then, the discussion of the five agenda items began. There was not much dispute from any side, and the meeting proceeded smoothly. At 11:15 AM, a temporary recess was announced, and the representatives went outside to stroll. Our reporter met with our representative, Mr. Cao Yunxiang, and inquired about the content of the morning's discussion. According to him, the morning's discussion focused on the various agenda items, which could all be completed today. As for the issue of the puppet organization's participation, the Japanese side had not yet raised it. Mr. Wang Zhengting was unable to come south to attend today's meeting due to official duties. It has always been customary for the three countries' Standing Committee meeting to be held before the General Assembly. The idea of a round table conference is a deliberate attempt to mislead, and our country should not be taken advantage of. When asked what attitude our representatives would take if the Japanese side raised the issue of the puppet organization, Mr. Cao replied that discussion is always possible, but our country's firm rejection has been repeatedly declared at home and abroad.

Informal Meeting: Japan Proposes Manchukuo

At 2:30 PM in the afternoon, the representatives gathered at the original location. Since all five agenda items had been completed, there was no need for further discussion, and an informal meeting was convened. Dr. Tambuatting of the Philippines remained as chairman. As soon as the meeting began, the Japanese representative Yamamoto raised the issue of the puppet organization's participation. His reason was based on the precedent of allowing India to participate in the performance at the 9th Far Eastern Games held in Tokyo in 1930. He repeatedly reiterated this and cited the General Assembly's regulations, distorting the reasons he held between the words and sentences of the charter. Yamamoto also stated that the puppet organization was requesting to participate in the performance and was not requesting to join as a member. Joining as a member requires the consent of all member countries. Yamamoto's words flowed incessantly, and after our representatives vehemently refuted this, the Japanese side continued to argue incessantly.

Yamamoto Suggests Postponement to This Morning

Finally, Yamamoto rose and suggested to the chairman, Dr. Tambuatting of the Philippines, that this issue was unusually complex, and each country had considerable opinions. Japan's Attitude is Aggressively Conservative

According to sources from the Japanese side, the Japanese side's proposal for the puppet organization to join the performance as a non-member already represents a concession. The Japanese sports world is divided into two factions on this issue: the aggressive and the conservative. The aggressive faction believes that if China does not recognize Manchuria's participation, a separate Far East Games should be convened. The conservative faction believes that this point involves political issues and is not of great value, and that Japan does not want to withdraw. Therefore, the future of this Far East Games depends on whether the Japanese can abandon their conspiracy. According to Professor Tambuatting, the Philippine representative, he told reporters that he had no opinion on the issue of the puppet organization's participation, but that he hoped everyone would be satisfied so that the future of this Far East Games would be bright and happy. He is preparing to return to the Philippines on the Asia Queen.

Respectfully inform our national representatives: The puppet organization's participation in the performance should be resolutely refused for discussion.

On the issue of the puppet organization's participation in the Far Eastern Games, our country, from the government to the people, has unanimously expressed a firm rejection. Overseas Chinese everywhere have also sent telegrams calling for it, and emotions are extremely high. Mr. Wang Zhengting and the authorities of the Sports Advancement Association have successively stated that they would rather be shattered jade than a whole tile, and that if the puppet organization participates in the General Assembly, they would withdraw immediately without hesitation. Yesterday, the Standing Committee meeting of the three countries (China, Japan, and the Philippines) opened in Shanghai. In the morning, all five agenda items were completed, and the task of the meeting was declared over. However, in the afternoon, a so-called informal meeting was suddenly convened. Our representatives did not object in advance, and after the Japanese side raised the issue of the puppet organization's participation, they allowed them to suggest to the chairman to allow them to postpone the meeting until this morning, which was already the first mistake, unknowingly falling into the Japanese side's meticulously arranged maze. The continuing meeting this morning is to discuss the entire issue of the puppet organization's participation, which is very clear. The Northeast is part of our country's territory and has no so-called special organization, let alone a nation. No matter which article in the charter the Japanese representative Yamamoto cites, it is absolutely not a reason. As for the precedent of India, it absolutely cannot be used for the puppet organization. In our opinion, since the agenda has been fully discussed and completed, there should be no more informal meetings, so that the Japanese side can easily raise this issue. Once they raise it, we should resolutely refuse to discuss it, and finally, we should not hesitate to withdraw from the meeting to conform to the spirit of unwavering determination repeatedly expressed by Mr. Wang Zhengting and other sports authorities. Instead of doing this, they agreed to continue participating in this morning's discussion. We sincerely hope that our representatives will uphold the personality of our nation and country, and it may not be too late to mend the fold after a sheep is lost. We respectfully wish you to use the most courageous spirit to resolutely refuse to discuss it and not fall for the other party's cunning schemes again.

Chen Diaoyuan Advances to Suppress Fang Zhimin's Bandits 丨Chen Has Led Troops to Anhui to Supervise Suppression丨 141

Jiujiang Correspondence: In order to increase the bandit suppression forces in the five provinces and to eliminate the bandit Fang Zhimin's band in the border areas of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Anhui within a limited time, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek specially requested the central government to appoint Chen Diaoyuan as the Commander-in-Chief of the Reserve Army for the Suppression of Communists in the Five Provinces of Jiangxi, Guangdong, Fujian, Hunan, and Hubei. After Chen officially took office on the first of this month, he discussed with Chairman Chiang a plan to eliminate the communist bandits in the border areas of northeastern Jiangxi, southwestern Zhejiang, and southeastern Anhui. Chen then led the headquarters of the Reserve Army and the First Route headquarters yesterday to Wuyuan to command the suppression. According to investigations, Fang Zhimin, a communist bandit in eastern Jiangxi, started his rebellion in 1927 with only a few defeated rifles and spears in the border area of Yiheng and Gui. Due to the incompetence of the stationed troops and local governments, he grew stronger day by day. By 1931, his fake Tenth Army commander Zhou Jianping had only nine companies of basic bandit troops. In 1932, Fang's bandits crossed the Xin River from southern Henan, passed through Shangqing Palace in Guixi, and joined forces with Peng's bandits who came east from southern Jiangxi. They also united with Zhu Mao's forces in southeastern Jiangxi. The puppet central government then appointed Fang as the commander-in-chief of the Seventh Army Corps, allocated weapons, and expanded his band into the 19th, 20th, 21st, and 3rd Armies. At the same time, two puppet military regions were established: Xiao Jingguang was appointed commander of the puppet Zhejiang-Jiangxi-Fujian Military Region, and Tang Yangan was appointed commander of the puppet Jiangxi-Zhejiang-Anhui Military Region. They recruited bandits in Guangxin counties and the border areas of Fujian, Zhejiang, and Anhui, and established so-called puppet independent regiments. Since then, the communist bandits in the border areas of Jiangxi, Fujian, Zhejiang, and Anhui have become like a long snake, fleeing from one place to another, and the border counties of the four provinces have been unable to rest easy. Recently, Fang's bandits have been using Hengfeng as their base. The puppet Northeast Revolutionary Committee, the puppet army corps headquarters, and all reactionary organizations are located there. Their bandit forces use Dexing and Hengfeng as their rear, the border area between Jiangxi and Fujian as their development area, and the border area between Zhejiang and Anhui as their guerrilla zone. Moreover, Fang's bandits regard Zhejiang as a wealthy area and frequently invade areas such as Suian, Kaihua, Jiangshan, and Changshan, resembling the early days of the bandit disaster in eastern Jiangxi in 1927 and 1928. The counties of Chong'an, Pucheng, and Guangze in northern Fujian are almost like the period of 1927 and 1928. Shangrao, Guixi, and Qianshan in eastern Jiangxi have become the lairs of these bandits. This time, Chairman Chiang has set a deadline for the elimination of communist bandits in various provinces. Large armies from the east, west, north and south are surrounding Zhu Mao in the Jiangxi-Fujian border area, and He Jian is responsible for suppressing Xiao Ke and Kong Hechong in western Jiangxi. Therefore, Chen Diaoyuan is responsible for eliminating Fang's bandits. At this moment, a large number of fresh troops have been transferred to the borders of Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Fujian, and Anhui, and they will unite to encircle and suppress the bandits, aiming to eradicate them as soon as possible. (April 6th)

Kailuan Coal Mine Strike Eases - The Process of Workers Surrounding the Commissioner's Office - Hebei Provincial Government Sets Three-Day Deadline for Resolution 142

Tianjin Correspondence: The Tangshan coal mine strike became tense when the Huaxin and Qixin strikes occurred. When the Huaxin workers were reinstated after the factory manager and officials worked together to mediate, the Qixin strike, when it first occurred, was handled well by the company and nipped in the bud. Only the Tangshan miners remained, the mine refusing to accept their conditions, work could not resume, and thus trouble arose. Now Zhao Dazhong has gradually lost the general faith of the workers, so the majority of the workers are urgently seeking to resume work to avoid financial difficulties, resulting in the act of surrounding the Commissioner's Office on April 3 to demand recognition of the conditions. Before the workers actually surrounded the office that day, Zhao Dazhong first went to the Commissioner's Office to meet with Tao Shangming, Zhao Xun, and Li Yinchun, the inspector stationed at the factory by the Hebei Construction Department, to request a response to the previously proposed conditions. After two hours of talks, no results were achieved. The workers waited for Zhao Dazhong at the Xuzhou Guild Hall, and seeing that Zhao had been gone for a long time and had not returned, they formed a team to go to the Commissioner's Office, claiming that they would not disperse if the conditions were not recognized. Initially, there were three to four hundred workers, but later it gradually gathered to six to seven hundred, blocking traffic. The workers also frequently chanted slogans. Zhao Dazhong then left the Commissioner's Office and gave a speech to the workers, telling them not to retreat without results. Unexpectedly, Zhao left immediately after the speech and never reappeared. The workers then elected eleven representatives to enter and meet with Tao Shangming, presenting two demands: (A) For the officials, (1) Allow the establishment of a Joint Affairs Office of the War Zone Workers' Union as a labor-management agency to manage labor-management affairs in the Luan-Yu area; (2) Overthrow all old trade unions in the counties within the war zone; (3) Overthrow all party organizations in the war zone; (B) For the mine, a total of ten items were proposed, the most important being the second and eighth items. The second item concerned the labor-management contract of 1931, which must be implemented immediately, and the eighth item demanded that the mine must immediately pay the wages during the strike period. Negotiations lasted another three hours, but still no progress was made. The eleven representatives withdrew and re-elected two representatives to enter and talk again, but still no results were achieved. At 11:00 pm, the workers did not retreat, and they elected seven people to enter the office again to contact Tao Shangming. Tao told the workers that he could not immediately respond to the official demands, and that he had to ask the higher authorities for instructions, and that the second and third demands concerned the entire war zone, and that the Luan-Yu administrative region had limited authority and had no right to respond on behalf of others. The workers' representatives expressed understanding that the second and third demands could be put on hold first, but the first item must be handled immediately, and a notice must be issued that night, and the conditions proposed by the workers to the mine must also be negotiated on their behalf and recognized immediately, otherwise the workers would never retreat. Tao contacted Gu Zhenxiang, the assistant manager of the Kailuan Mining Bureau in Tianjin, by telephone, but Gu said that the mine would never reward the workers for resuming work under any conditions, and in the end there was no result. It is estimated that the workers started the siege from 5:00 pm on the 3rd and were unwilling to leave until 3:00 am on the 4th. Fearing that the workers would have a change of heart, Li Yinchun discussed the plan with Zhao Dazhong over the phone for a long time and decided on a solution: (1) Li Yinchun is responsible for contacting the conditions; (2) Zhao Dazhong led the workers back to the trade union to wait for news. If no one from the mining bureau comes at noon on the 5th, further action will be taken. After the plan was decided, Zhao Dazhong went to the front of the Commissioner's Office at about 4:00 am on the 4th and led the workers to retreat.

The old Guangdong Street trade union held a meeting and dismissed at about 6:00 am. On the 5th, Tangshan kept calling to urge the mining bureau to send personnel to Tang to talk with the workers, but the mining bureau was determined not to accept any conditions. By the evening, the workers saw that no one from the mining bureau had arrived, and they planned to surround the Commissioner's Office again. Upon hearing the news, Tao Shangming hurriedly sent someone to the trade union to dissuade them, promising to urge the mining bureau representatives to come to Tang again. On the same day, the workers learned that Yu Xuezhong had returned to Tianjin and would take strict measures against the mine strike. At the same time, after the Qixin resumed work, the workers did not participate in the strike movement, and the various mines were in financial difficulties due to the long strike, and Zhao Dazhong's tricks of deceiving the workers were gradually exposed, so they did not take active action. The Tangshan gentry took the opportunity to mediate between the officials, mines, and workers, and a peaceful solution was in progress. The order from the Hebei Provincial Government had also arrived in Tang, strictly prohibiting illegal activities by workers at the request of the mining bureau, and setting a three-day deadline for the Commissioner's Office to resolve the mine strike and arrest Zhao Dazhong and send him to Tianjin for trial. At this point, the workers' attitude turned softer, and as of tonight (the 7th), there is hope of pacification. (7th)

Restaurant Employee Dies in Car Accident 146

Hu Yulin, the driver of business car No. 684 of the Linji Business Car Company on Tonghui Road, drove passengers to Xiaoji Mountain for sightseeing at 11:00 am yesterday (the 8th). The car stopped after passing through Meiyuan. At that time, Kong Jigen (35 years old), a restaurant employee from Xiaoji Mountain, also intended to take the car to Xiaoji Mountain for business. The driver Hu Yulin agreed to let him get in the car. When the car reached the vicinity of the Second Peak of Wanyuan Hall, Kong Jigen's food plate suddenly fell to the ground. As the car was speeding, Kong Jigen immediately pushed open the car door, intending to pick it up. Unexpectedly, he accidentally fell out of the car and lost consciousness. Lü Shiqiao Acquitted on Retrial 147

Tan Qixuan, the former Director of the Administrative Bureau in northern Wuxi County, was shot and killed by bandits in April 1929. After Tan Zhong, the father of the deceased, reported the case to the county government, he successively arrested the persons involved in the case, including Guo Asi, Zhu Ada, Zeng Axing, Lü Shiqiao, and Lü Genhu, and brought them to justice. Except for Zeng Axing, Guo Asi, and Zhu Ada, who had been sentenced to death and executed by shooting, Lü Shiqiao and Lü Genhu were sentenced to death by the former Wuxi County Government for the crime of premeditated murder. Later, Lü Shiqiao appealed to the High Court, which acquitted him. The prosecutor of the High Court then appealed to the Supreme Court, which sent the case back to the High Court for retrial. Hu Shan, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division of the Suzhou High Court, has now concluded the trial and declared Lü Shiqiao and Lü Genhu not guilty.

Changzhou: Parricide Case Occurs in Benniu Town 149

Zhang Changgen, a 61-year-old man in Xidu, Benniu Town, Wuyi County, makes a small business to make a living. Because he is old and weak, he must rest for a while every afternoon before he can go out. Unexpectedly, his son Suobao did not allow his father to rest at noon on the 8th, and forced him to go out to do business immediately. Zhang Changgen did not answer, but Suobao took a knife and slashed at his head, causing serious injuries and bleeding profusely. He also threw the utensils, kerosene lamp, and rice bowl to the ground. Fortunately, he was stopped by bystanders, and Zhang Changgen was able to escape to the Public Security Second Branch in the town to report. Zhou Daonan, the director of the bureau, believed that the case was a parricide and injury to a parent, so he sent police to arrest the rebellious son Zhang Suobao, held a preliminary trial, and Zhang Suobao confessed to slashing his old father and requested leniency. Director Zhou of the Branch Bureau immediately sent the rebellious son and his father to the General Bureau in the city for review. The General Bureau ordered Zhang Changgen to be treated quickly because his injuries were quite serious, and transferred the rebellious son to the County Court Procuratorate for interrogation on the 9th.

Japan Observation Record of the Chinese Child Education Society - A Short Stay in Kobe 152

(II)

— Zhou Shang

(Kobe Correspondence) On April 2nd at 5:00 pm, we bid farewell to Nagasaki. The voyage was smoother than before, so the passengers in the boat were bustling and talking intimately. Japanese also came to greet the residents. Many of them talked about the Far Eastern Games and knew our country's lineup very well. They think that we have hopefuls in athletics (1) Chen Baoqiu (Discus), (2) Situ Guang (Triple Jump), (3) Liu Changchun (Sprint), (4) Jin Zhongkang (Long Distance), (5) Fu Bao (Pole Vault). Each newspaper also competed to record and predict, and said that Mr. Fu is a staff member of the Diligent Bookstore, and Diligent is the only sports bookstore in China. Is their survey clear? I wonder if we can compete with them.

At 3:00 pm on the 3rd, the boat arrived in Kobe. First, there was an inquiry by the Water Police, and then an inquiry by the Customs. Fortunately, we are a visiting group. The Kobe City Government and our country's consulate sent people to greet us, and there was no kind of detour. After landing, we stayed at the late night hostel in Bu Street 1-chome. The hostel is completely Japanese style and exceptionally clean, but there is a kind of smell in the nest, which is the so-called "Japanese smell". At first, it makes people cover their noses for a short time, and then it becomes a habit. All the women in the hostel are serving. These women have received at least six years of elementary school education, which shows that their national education is very vigorous.

As soon as the hostel was settled, Consul General Lin Yanfang, Chairman of the Chinese Association Zhan Daying, Manager of Osaka China Bank Jie Kexie, and Director of Chinese Public School Dong Gong successively visited. During the banquet, the situation of overseas Chinese in Japan was mentioned, which is worthy of warning. It is said that there are three areas for overseas Chinese in Japan: Tokyo, where there are many students, Osaka, and Kobe, all of which are businessmen. The number of people in Osaka is less than one-third of Kobe, and they are all temporary in nature, mostly Shanghai branch stores. Kobe overseas Chinese are like natives, some of whom have lived there for generations, and some of whom have been in Japan for fifty or sixty years. There are more than 5,000 people. Wu Jintang is the richest among the overseas Chinese, with assets of more than 10 million. Unfortunately, he has joined the Japanese nationality. After the "January 28th" Incident, the number of overseas Chinese has sharply decreased, now about 2,000, and all of them are about to go bankrupt and are in a precarious state. The reason is that domestic goods are resisted, and the overseas Chinese sell goods to the natives in Nanyang, so the market has stopped. In the meantime, this kind of benefit has been taken away by the Japanese. Ninety percent of Japanese goods (more than 200 million gold) are operated by overseas Chinese, and now only 10% are left. Major goods are sold directly by the Japanese. When we heard the news, we could only swallow our voices and hesitate and could not speak.

The Japanese have been strictly suppressing Chinese workers since the earthquake. Recently, under the pretext of not allowing them to land, those who were ordered to return to their country are everywhere. Therefore, poor Chinese who come here must prepare round-trip travel expenses and deposit half of them in the Japanese consulate in Shanghai as travel expenses for returning. However, they can still mix with cargo ships, waters, and cargo teams to land. By the time they enter the inland, the Japanese police can't detect it. There are currently more than 2,000 Chinese workers in Tokyo, mostly engaged in digging ditches and carrying goods. This work is not even willing to be done by Koreans and Taiwanese, but our Chinese workers are doing it well. Who said that Chinese people are not as hardworking as others? There are still many Chinese merchants selling cloth, noodles, hairdressing, and Western clothes in Hanshin, but recently because the Japanese like Chinese noodles, the Japanese are strongly repelling them, which has become a problem. There are now about hundreds of people, and I don't know how to solve it in the future. There are about 1,000 Chinese hairdressers. The Japanese examination for hairdressers is very strict. All aspects of technology, hygiene, and methods are subject to inspection one by one. After passing the exam, if other barber shops on the same street do not agree or the number of households in a street has not reached a certain limit, it is difficult to obtain the qualification to open a barber shop. There are currently hundreds of Western clothing merchants, which can be said to be free. Among the overseas Chinese, those residing in Kobe are mostly from Sanjiang (Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Jiangxi), while those in Osaka are mostly from Dalian, Yingkou, Tianjin, and northern compatriots. The Chinese Association in Shin-Osaka is the general organization of the overseas Chinese. It has self-built houses, which are magnificent and impressive. I hope to work hard to create more benefits for the overseas Chinese.

▲ Kobe City Education Administration Organization

Kobe is a transit point for tourists, and not many people in our country have the opportunity to visit for a long time. This Jiangsu Education Inspection Team only stayed for three hours. We have a short stay of two days, and the observation points should be different. Now, please first describe the general situation of its education administration organization for your reference. The city has a population of 820,200 people, but no education bureau. All educational undertakings in the city are handled by the Education Section of the municipal government. There is one section chief, four principals, four inspectors, three school health doctors, twenty-two clerks, supplementary clerks, employees, and servants, and three youth training staff, totaling thirty-seven people. The division of their affairs is: one is the academic affairs department, which is the same as the academic affairs section of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau; the second is the manager department, which manages the school's economy; the third is the construction department, which is responsible for school construction; the fourth is the general affairs department, which handles external visits and other miscellaneous affairs; and the fifth is the social education department, which includes youth training centers, women's associations, libraries, and strong men's education surveys.

The improvement of education in the city is discussed and evaluated by the Academic Affairs Committee, and opinions are submitted to the government for approval. The city has ten members of the Academic Affairs Committee, four of whom are members of the city council, four of whom are elected by the citizens of the city, and two of whom are male teachers in municipal elementary schools. I don't know why female teachers do not have this qualification.

The city's annual education expenditure is 1,320,000 yuan, and the expenditure is 6,022,000 yuan. The numbers are not small, and should be subsidized by the city government. The distribution of funds for various schools is as follows: (1) Elementary schools 2,998,364 yuan, night schools 2,901 yuan, vocational schools 182,822 yuan, kindergartens 61,579 yuan, secondary schools 358,307 yuan, libraries 41,112 yuan, youth training centers 53,957 yuan, and sports field fees 16,625 yuan.

Regarding the comparison of class size, children's population, number of households, city income, and education expenditure, the main points are described as follows:

Developing Northwest Culture - Board Meeting of Luoyang Experimental Zone - Yu Qingtang Reports on Preparation Process 153

In order to develop the culture of the Northwest and awaken the people, the Chinese Social Education Society specially joined forces with the Education Department of the Henan Provincial Government and the Luoyang County Government to form the Luoyang Experimental Zone. On the 3rd of this month, the board of directors was held in the Luoyang Central Plains Social Education Museum to discuss the implementation methods. The details of the society's initiation process and the meeting situation are recorded below.

Origin of Initiation 154

When the society convened the fourth board meeting in the capital last year (1933) in March, there was a "proposal to prepare a mass education experimental zone." It was immediately resolved that "Zhao Yantao, Chen Dabai, Gao Jianji, etc. should draft concrete methods and submit them to the next board meeting for discussion. The location of the zone should be near Luoyang to facilitate contact with the Central Plains Social Education Museum to develop social education in the Central Plains." Since the proposal was passed, they started contacting and preparing separately. In May, Niu Yangsheng, the Deputy Dean of the Examination Yuan, came to Luoyang and inspected the social situation in the countryside, selected the experimental area, and drafted an outline of the Luoyang Mass Education Experimental Zone plan, which was sent to the Chinese Social Education Society on May 16. Gao Jianji expressed his opinions, and Zhao Guangtao was appointed to survey the location of the zone. Zhao, along with Yang Rubing and four others, went to Baimasi Pingyue Village and other places from Xu to Luoyang on June 5 for inspection and called on the village leaders of Baimasi to talk and conduct a simple general survey. After the inspection, he returned to Luoyang and invited the leaders of the political and educational circles in Luoyang to report on the significance and plan of establishing the experimental zone, and the discussion was very pleasant. In August, when the society held its second annual meeting, the Jiangsu Provincial Xuzhou Mass Education Museum proposed "actively preparing the Luoyang Mass Education Experimental Zone." It was immediately revised and passed, and the board of directors appointed Niu Tiesheng, Gao Yang, Zhao Guangtao, Wang Haihan, and Chen Dabai to organize a design committee and appointed Niu Tiesheng to convene and carry out the design work of the experimental zone. Later, the society believed that the promotion of social education in the country was needed in all provinces, so it contacted the Henan Education Department and the Luoyang County Government to discuss and cooperate. Subsequently, the society drafted the Luoyang Mass Education Experimental Zone Measures and Plan Outline, convened a symposium of directors in Wuxi, discussed and decided on two documents, and sent letters to the preparatory committee to express their opinions and revised them again. It also consulted with the Henan Education Department and the Luoyang County Government on the measures and plan outline, hired directors, and convened the first board meeting. On the day of the meeting, all the directors participated from afar.

Attendees 155

There were Qi Zhenru (Director of the Henan Education Department), Wang Cifu (Administrative Commissioner of the 10th District of Henan and County Magistrate of Luoyang), Wang Weifan (Director of the Luoyang County Education Bureau), Zheng Ruogu (Dean of the Faculty of Arts of Henan University), Song Xiangzhou Zhao Mian (Representative of Chen Dabai), Zhao Guangtao (Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Xuzhou Mass Education Museum), Guo Fangwu (Director of the Luoyang Orphanage), Niu Yongjian (Deputy Dean of the Examination Yuan), Yu Qingtang (Executive Director of the Chinese Social Education Society), Wang Haihan (Section Chief of the Third Section of the Henan Education Department), and eleven others. Niu Yongjian was appointed as the chairman, Chen Dabai recorded, and after the etiquette, Yu Qingtang reported on the preparation process of the experimental zone and the measures and plan outline of the zone. Later, because there were too many proposals, Qi Zhenru was re-appointed as the chairman at 2:00 pm to continue the discussion. The important ones

Resolutions 156

(1) Regarding how to decide on the name of the experimental district, it was resolved that the district be named the "Henan Provincial Department of Education, China Social Education Society, and Luoyang County Government Jointly Established Luoyang Experimental District." (2) Regarding where the Luoyang Experimental District should be located, it was resolved that the district's location be within the third district of Luoyang, selecting the most suitable village as the basic educational area. (3) Regarding whether the Luoyang Experimental District should first appoint a chief instructor and establish a preparatory office, it was resolved to appoint Chen Dabai as the chief instructor and establish a preparatory office, with the chief instructor concurrently serving as the director of the preparatory office. (4) Regarding the submission of the outline of the preparatory period plan and the budget for public decision, it was resolved to pass it as amended in the original proposal. (5) Regarding how to raise funds during the preparatory period, it was resolved that the start-up costs would be raised separately by Director Niu, Director-General Qi, Commissioner Wang, and others, and the recurring expenses would be shared by the Henan Provincial Department of Education, the Luoyang County Government, and the China Social Education Society. (6) Regarding the submission of the outline of the district's first-year plan for public decision, it was resolved to pass it as reviewed. (7) Regarding whether the executive directors of the association should appoint an annual director to take special responsibility, it was resolved to appoint the annual directors in the following rotating order: first and fourth years, China Social Education Society; second and fifth years, Henan Provincial Department of Education; third and sixth years, Luoyang County Government. (8) Regarding how the joint establishment authorities should allocate responsibilities for implementation, it was resolved to hand it over to the executive directors for consideration. (9) Regarding whether the board of directors of the association should be increased, it was resolved to increase the number of expert directors to four to six and the number of local directors to two to four. (10) Regarding when the preparatory work should begin, it was resolved to begin immediately. (11) Regarding when the second board meeting should be held, it was resolved to be held in Kaifeng on August 16th.

Wang Ruibing Invents Six-Color Automatic Scientific Writing Method; Currently Experimenting in Ningbo Primary Schools; Will Give Public Lectures in Shanghai Soon 161

Mr. Wang Ruibing of Ningbo recently invented a six-color automatic scientific writing method. Its function is to enable illiterate people to learn to write on their own by following the guidance of different colors, and to understand the preliminary meaning and structure of words through this method. It is truly a shortcut to assisting the future of popular education in our country. Mr. Wang is now carrying all the charts, etc., to conduct on-site experiments in the primary schools of the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Townsmen Association. He will give public lectures soon. Yesterday, the Shanghai social reporter

contacted Mr. Wang to discuss the invention process and the content of the writing method as follows:

Invention Process 162

Mr. Wang has been devoted to mass education in Zhejiang Province for many years. Recently, in view of the importance of popular education in our country, the Chinese people have been sparing no effort in promoting literacy campaigns in recent years. However, most civilians who aspire to literacy are often limited by economic, time, space, and other factors, and cannot achieve their aspirations. Therefore, adhering to the principle that "if one can write, one can recognize," after seven years of research and practical experimentation, he invented the six-color automatic scientific writing method. In about a week, it can enable illiterate people to write and copy Chinese characters without making mistakes in strokes, and the style can be correct, and they can understand the structure of the characters. It is said to be a shortcut to promoting literacy campaigns.

Content Description 163

The six-color automatic scientific writing method uses six colors to distribute each character or each character in each square grid, and arranges these six characters in a certain order, namely, the first "red", the second "orange", the third "yellow", the fourth "green", the fifth "blue", and the sixth "purple". Using this writing method, there is no need for painstaking guidance from education. As long as the learner remembers the order of colors and the two sentences "from top to bottom" and "from left to right," according to the thickness, length, size, the learner moves by himself, there will be no errors. The book has not yet been published, but there are sample sheets and instructions available for reference.

Field Testing 164

According to Mr. Wang, the original manuscript of this book has been reviewed by many educational experts such as Cai Yuanpei, Tao Zhixing, Chen Heqin, Hu Shuyi, Shen Baiying, and Lin Zhuoran. After coming to Shanghai, he has given lectures and speeches at the Youth Association, Ningbo Fellow Townsmen Association, and other places, which have been very popular in society. In addition to conducting field experiments in the main schools of the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Townsmen Association, he is also drawing detailed diagrams and writing instructions, and plans to hold a grand public promotion on a scheduled date in the near future, and use the results of the experiment to carry out a national literacy campaign.

Essay Contest for Archeology Award; Organized by the Science Society of China 165

The essay contest for the archeology award is organized by the Science Society of China in Shanghai. It has been held once a year since 1930, giving it to one of the best researchers in the field of archeology in the country. This award is donated by members in Beijing. In addition to a cash prize of 100 yuan, the winner will also receive a gold medal to commemorate the event. To be solemn, the society has appointed Mr. Weng Wenhao, Ding Wenjiang, and Zhang Hongzhao as members of the archeology award committee to be responsible for the handling. Anyone in the country who has made new discoveries in archeology can write a paper and send it to the society for application. It is heard that the winner of the previous award was Mr. Pei Wenzhong, who discovered the skull of Peking Man.

Academic Lectures of the Modern Thought Society 166

The Modern Thought Society has organized modern thought lectures to popularize modern academic thought. For the first and second lectures, Mr. Tao Baichuan and Pan Gongzhan were invited to speak successively. It is learned that for the third lecture, Mr. Tong Xingbai, a member of the Standing Committee of the Municipal Party Department, will be invited to speak on the topic "The New Life Movement and the Revival of the Nation." The location and date will be announced temporarily. It has also been recently decided by the society to continue recruiting members. The contact point is Mr. Wang Longzhang of the Municipal Party Department.

The Serious Situation in North China Causes a Sudden and Sharp Drop in Public Bonds; Only Three Trading Sessions Were Completed, Closing at 7 PM; Declines Ranging from Slightly Over One Yuan to More Than Three Yuan 173

Yesterday, April 9th, the public bond market experienced an extremely turbulent day. The gains accumulated over the past few days were almost entirely wiped out in a single day. This was a natural consequence of events, but the speed was unexpected. The main reasons for this are Huang Fu's southward journey, the deadlock in negotiations in North China, the rampant behavior of Japanese troops in North China, a decline in public confidence compared to before, the dispersal of bullish forces, small investors rushing to sell, northern speculators engaging in short selling, and many large investors seeing the unfavorable trend and also selling off. As a result, the first session in the morning saw a small decline of several jiao (tenths of a yuan) to 1.5 or 1.6 yuan. The rebound was indeed not significant. Although the second session saw very little fluctuation, investor sentiment was poor. Only the aggressive buying of No. 46 barely managed to stabilize the market. After the evening newspaper was published, news of impending negotiations between China and Japan and the secret transportation of Japanese troops to China further eroded confidence. Coupled with the frantic selling by Northern firms like No. 11, the market became increasingly weak, with each bond falling another 7 or 8 jiao to 1.5 or 1.6 yuan. Oil Market: The Price of Hankou White Tung Oil Accelerates Upwards 184

The price of white tung oil in the Hankou market is gradually rising. Initially, the momentum was not too strong, but recently there has been a clear trend of soaring prices. At the beginning of this month, foreign firms were still selling at 25 yuan. In the following three or four days, the telegram price had already increased to 26 yuan, and on the seventh day, the telegram price was 27 yuan. Last night, the telegram price from Hankou increased again to 27.6 yuan, and further increases are expected. In just one week, the price has risen by about 3 yuan. The intensity of the price increase is unprecedented in recent years. The transaction volume is about 1,000 tons. When the price was at 24 or 25 yuan, foreign firms only handled a few dozen or a hundred tons at most, so it was difficult to say that the price increase was gradual, and the momentum was not too strong. When the price was between 26 and 27 yuan, there were a total of 500 or 600 tons of transactions, which created a market of rapid and aggressive price increases. However, the supply is still scarce, and there is a shortage of goods. Recently, Hankou purchased Xiang tung oil at prices ranging from 20.078 to 21.56 yuan, and supported tung oil was also increased from 21 to about 23 yuan. These are all customer prices. Foreign firms in this port also purchased several dozen tons in the previous week, but because they rely on Zhejiang tung oil, they could not sell in large quantities. Seeing the continuous price increases in the Hankou market, the Hangzhou market also followed suit and increased prices. Two or three days ago, the price was still only 21.46 yuan per dan (a unit of weight) delivered to Shanghai. According to yesterday's telegram, the price has been raised to 22 yuan. Local firms, recognizing that this price increase is entirely driven by foreign sales, while domestic sales remain the same, are not too enthusiastic about purchasing from Hangzhou and are only buying and selling as needed.

Free Talk

Revenge 189

— Charles

Eastern culture has generally been influenced by the doctrine of benefitting the world, and everything is explained in ethical terms, adding a stinking odor of education, thus neglecting the true reality of life. In other words, life has been worn down and destroyed. Everyone has spent two thousand years in a low-level education system.

Therefore, anyone who breaks the rules or reforms the status quo has become a madman, a genius, or a hermit. Buddhism does not center on humanity but longs for another world, yet it has passed on the Avici hell to people in this world. Common people are the embodiment of great rebellious thought and revolutionary thought. Compassion is a powerful weapon, non-resistance is actually the greatest resistance, and benevolence is often the greatest revenge!

For example, an eye for an eye and a tooth for a tooth is the simplest thing. However, if one can forgive, tolerate, and influence even an enemy, then the enemy will suffer the greatest pain. Because as long as one is human, one must have human feelings and a sense of conscience and ability. The Greeks understood this best, so the torture in hell depicted in their mythology is not a mountain of knives or a forest of swords, but a simple scourging of "conscience"! The suffering in life surpasses all punishment!

The Buddha's saying that the Buddha's power subdues lions and elephants, and tames dragons and tigers, is actually the best allegory!

Cold-blooded people, with poisonous flames filling the sky, usurp benevolence and righteousness, becoming great traitors, almost making the land barren. There are so many such people in history, but they disappear like smoke when they encounter compassion, just as one can resist ten thousand men but cannot withstand the slight smile of a child. Human power is limited, but intention is boundless? The Story of the Investiture of the Gods tells how the magic treasures of many demons and monsters are shattered into dust when they encounter the brilliance of the Tathagata. Although this is a foolish tale, it does indeed look down upon the demons in the world, feeling that they are nothing, and so it is written.

Although this may seem like a form of empty spiritual victory, it is not. Only revenge with compassion is truly victorious and permanently overcomes. Without spiritual victory first, there will never be material victory. The true reality of life is pure and peaceful, like the radiance of the sky. It is full of compassion and joy, and any darkness or malice will disappear without a trace when they encounter it. Is this not the greatest revenge?

The Emperor's Majesty 190

— Le Bao

"The six armies did not advance, what could be done? The beautiful face was turned away, and she died before the horses." Let me say a word to the emperor!

The woman widened her slender eyes, shooting terrifying beams to the left and right. The warriors pulling her involuntarily took a step back. She lifted the red silk skirt that was dragging on the ground, raised her proud face, and rushed straight to the chariot drawn by three fine horses. Just as she was about to say:

"Your Majesty, how can you let them act so violently?"

But when she saw the emperor sitting in the chariot, his face had already turned pale, and the gray-white beard hanging on the front of his yellow robe was trembling incessantly (this was something she had never seen or imagined), she stamped her foot angrily and said:

"Old man, you've simply forgotten that you're an emperor! Hurry up and show the majesty of an emperor!"

When the emperor saw that his concubine was still so valiant, and the shouts around had stopped, he suddenly shouted instinctively:

"Yes, I almost forgot! Executioners, seize those troublemakers for me! You may ride with me in the chariot!"

The woman was about to climb into the chariot, and the emperor reached out to help her, but the voices around immediately clamored up, more fierce and terrifying than before. At the same time, a fully armed general rushed to the front of the chariot and said urgently: "Absolutely: Your Majesty! The revolution has come before the horses! Quickly: Quickly: "

The emperor scolded the general:

"I'm not afraid! I'm not afraid! See if they have the guts to kill an emperor!"

The general leaned down in the chariot and said in a panic:

"Your Majesty! This is not like being in the palace!"

"Does an emperor not worth half a cent in the wild?"

The emperor roared. The general was angry in his heart, but he just murmured:

"Listen, if we go on like this, we'll all be dead! What's the point of talking about being worth money or not!"

The woman leaned against the chariot, weeping as she stomped her feet, and complained loudly:

"Marrying an unfortunate peasant is more promising than you, better than you!"

The emperor was very annoyed by these stinging words, and hearing the increasingly fierce shouts, there were even one or two cries of "Kill the fatuous emperor", he suddenly shouted at the general:

"Then quickly announce my decree to them and have her executed on the spot without delay!"

The shouts immediately stopped after the decree was announced.

The woman struggled in the hands of the warriors, her beautiful face turned pale, bit her lip and cursed:

"The words spoken in the Hall of Eternal Life were all lies!"

The emperor closed his eyes tightly, and hot tears welled up from the corners of his eyes.

Fisherman 191

— Qiao Min

Thirty-six thousand hectares of misty water is your workplace for making a living. Taking a small boat, cast out your large net. Watching the waves of the lake, carrying your infinite hope. From sunset to moonset, from childhood to old age, you never dare to be frivolous. However, what you have earned is only half a lifetime of hunger and a lifetime of desolation.

In and Out of the Bathhouse 192

— Jiaming

The steam filled the room, like a mist, like a light gauze.

Through this light gauze, I watched the newly arrived guest.

He had a mass of white flesh all over, a full chest, full thighs. A thick mop of black hair covered his round head. Thick black eyebrows, and thick black short hair. His face seemed kind and amiable.

Coincidentally, he was standing directly across from me in the bathing cubicle.

I had no intention of developing any relationship with him, but just as I was lathering my hair with soap and turned on the tap, I suddenly shivered and drew my head back. Because, for some reason, the hot water was gone, and only cold water was pouring down!

The guest standing across from me, like me, was doused with cold water. So, we both involuntarily complained about the bathhouse attendant, and we began to chat.

"The equipment in this bathhouse is really terrible, things like this happen all the time," my new acquaintance said with a slight sigh.

"Ah, yes," I said, huddled to one side, rubbing my soap-covered hair, letting the cold water splash on the floor, "It's really infuriating when it's suddenly hot and cold like this!"

The water got hot again. I rinsed my hair, letting the water run over my body, and exchanged bits and pieces of conversation with him.

Just as the water's temperature gradually increased, we quickly became very friendly with each other. We stood facing each other naked, without any reservations, casually playing with whatever words we could think of, as if we were familiar friends.

He told me many things about bathhouses. He seemed to have been to every bathhouse in the city. His words sometimes contained amusing stories, but at other times they were a bit like an adventurous detective novel. After he recounted the story of how a teaboy in a bathhouse cleverly hid a guest's money bag, but was eventually discovered by the guest, he said in a very gentle, sighing tone,

"It's such a terrible thing, one even has to be careful to protect their money bag while bathing."

So, we both sighed in mutual sympathy about the treacherousness of people's hearts in society today, and talked about many other aspects of life in society.

We talked very enthusiastically. I learned that his surname was Yu and that he was a small businessman. I also let him know my name and profession.

The steam thickened again. Through this gauze, I saw my new acquaintance sticking his head out, holding a wet towel.

"Finished?" I asked.

"Finished, I'll go out first." He ran his hand through the water on his hair. "Are you going anywhere after you finish washing?" (To be continued)

### Tentative Translation of the Book of Odes 193

— Yushi Xia

The Guofeng Gaoyou Chapter of the State of Gui

One

Wearing a lambskin coat, strolling leisurely,

Wearing a fox fur coat, to the court I go.

Is it that I don't think of you?

It makes my heart troubled!

Two

Wearing a lambskin coat, coming and going,

Wearing a fox fur coat, to the court I come.

Is it that I don't think of you?

It makes my heart sad!

Three

The lambskin coat is smooth as ointment,

When the sun comes out, it shines brightly.

Is it that I don't think of you?

It makes my heart grieve!

### Sketches of Beiping (6) Wowo Tou (Continued) 194

— Yao Ke

The dust that scrapes the ground falls on the stalls, sticking to all kinds of food. When cars pass by, the soup pots seem to have been sprinkled with a layer of pepper. These are things that "wowo tou eaters" don't care about, or even if they do, they can't do anything about it. Some people say that they have strong resistance and won't get sick or die even if they eat some dirt: this is really insightful, really right!

Once, a friend and I, with the determination to eat wowo tou, mustered up all our courage and went to a small street stall. We had just wanted to sit down awkwardly when suddenly a gust of wind swept up, covering the entire stall with dust. We looked at each other, our courage halved; just as the dust settled, a car sped past and stirred up another gust. We didn't dare sit down anymore and had to go to a restaurant a bit more upscale than the stall to try the taste of wowo tou.

Inside the door was a U-shaped counter, very short but very wide. Outside the counter were long benches, densely packed with hungry wolves of diners. The counter was covered with bowls and dishes in a jumble, a row of dishes containing pickles and oil-vinegar, and a large chopstick holder next to a large flat basket of pancakes and wowo tou. In the center of the counter was a stove boiling a large copper pot of millet porridge, and three waiters were busy darting around.

We ordered a plate of wowo tou, half a catty of sesame pancakes, and a plate of mung bean sprouts, and squeezed into the crowd to sit down. Breaking open the wowo tou, there was a burst of corn fragrance, and it tasted a bit sweet, but it was dry and coarse and really hard to swallow. We managed to get a large bowl of noodle soup to help us eat the plate. We only ate two-thirds of the sesame pancake, and sipped a small bowl of millet porridge, our stomachs were so full we couldn't eat anymore. Stealing glances at the other diners, we saw that their eyes were fixed on the food in the bowls and plates in front of them, and the muscles on the sides of their jaws | the so-called "masseter muscles" | were moving like the axles on a train wheel. The entire wowo tou seemed to turn into soft candy as soon as it reached their mouths, disappearing without a trace in an instant.

This is the proper, typical way to eat wowo tou; this is what I never knew, never carefully observed! Their way of eating is definitely not our ordinary way. When we eat, we focus on chewing and tasting; they focus on swallowing and stuffing. So, what we seek is the exquisite of the dishes; what they seek is the coarseness and solidity of the food, making sure it's stuffed full, lasts long, and is not easily digested! In our view, the purpose of eating is "nourishment"; in their view, the purpose of eating is "fueling up"!

In Beihai Park, there is a "Fangshan Restaurant" opened by chefs from the former Qing imperial kitchen, who make a kind of "wowo tou" the size of chestnuts | said to be what the emperors used to eat | with an exquisite style and a refined taste, sweet and melt-in-your-mouth, without even needing to chew, just tasting. This is only for serving the emperor; the working class definitely won't eat this kind of wowo tou.

### Half a Day of Lessons (7) 195

— Li Huiying

"The Governor has arrived."

"Governor."

Hearing others say it, I knew that the person who came was the great traitor Xi Qia. This hateful thing, he sold Jilin Province, sold all the fathers and elders of Jilin Province, no, he sold the entire Northeast to Japanese imperialism!

The military band played military music for him for a particularly long time, the military police paid him a grand salute, and Japanese elementary school students, led by their teachers, even shouted "Long live Governor Xi!" three times in a row!

There were more police, they originally said they were here to maintain order, but in fact, it was more like they were here to monitor the masses. They were a group of pitiful running dogs, and we were a group of pitiful slaves.

At nine o'clock, someone on the stage rang a bell, announcing the start of the meeting. Immediately afterward, three earth-shattering firecrackers were set off. Everyone naturally focused their attention on the stage.

"National flag raising ceremony."

This was the second item on the agenda, and after seeing it, I felt like my eyes were really blinded by sand: what's called a flag raising ceremony? I thought, this is probably a Japanese phrase, it should mean raising the national flag, right? Then, why mark it like this? Is it to assimilate people, or to deliberately please people in order to gain their favor?

Two national flags were raised at the same time. I don't understand why every time there is a meeting to raise the flag, there is always a Japanese flag. This situation was not present at the meeting two years ago. That sun flag, round and red, isn't it sucking blood from the people of the Northeast!

The master of ceremonies shouted the third item on the agenda:

"Bow three times to the national flag."

The more I thought about it, the angrier I got, and I didn't even bend my waist.

Then it was time to sing the national anthem. To tell the truth, after being a "Manchukuo" student for two years, I still can't sing the national anthem. The reason is because sadness and shame pressed down on my throat. I don't sing, I can't sing; but I can't stop others from singing, so I still have to listen to others humming the lyrics written by Old Man Zheng:

"Between heaven and earth, there is a new Manzhou;

New Manzhou, is the new world;

Standing tall, without sorrow or worry,

Creating our country,

Only love, no resentment!

The people are thirty million, the people are thirty million,

Even if it is multiplied tenfold, we will still be free!

Respecting benevolence and valuing etiquette, improving ourselves.

The family is in order, the country is governed, what else do we seek?

Close, we assimilate with the world,

Far, we flow with heaven and earth."

Talking Points

Eradicating Superstition or Promoting Superstition? 196

— Mengruo

The Chinese have always revered superstition, and have been poisoned by it for thousands of years. Since the import of new European and American ideas, the clamor to eradicate superstition stirred up a temporary storm. By the time the National Revolutionary Army had unified the north and south, all cultural relics and systems were tending towards innovation, and superstition was also on the list of things to be eliminated. At that time, a group of radical revolutionary youth went everywhere to destroy temples and smash idols, and the forces of superstition almost lost their footing. However, superstitious thoughts had already taken deep root in the minds of the general populace; therefore, despite your shouting to overthrow superstition, it still exists to this day. In addition, the current China is gradually showing signs of returning to the past; the embers of superstition will naturally reignite. For example, according to recent newspaper reports, Shanghai residents held a grand City God Festival during Qingming Festival. Upon hearing this news, the Municipal Government, in order to uphold its long-standing advocacy of eradicating superstition (?), immediately issued a joint announcement by the Public Security Bureau and the Social Affairs Bureau, strongly prohibiting it; saying that "welcoming gods and holding temple fairs is a waste of public money and promotes superstition, and should be suppressed according to previous cases," calling on the people "not to violate it deliberately, lest it cause inconvenience." On the one hand, we can understand that the people's thoughts are still as stubborn as ever, and on the other hand, we can also see that the authorities' determination to overthrow superstition has not diminished.

However, things in the world are always so farcical and interesting. At present, the most eye-catching major events in our country's society, apart from the New Life Movement advocated by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, are the Kalachakra initiation presided over by the Panchen Lama. This event was previously held in Beiping; this time, taking advantage of the National Teacher's trip to the south, at the proposal of important officials of the National Government and with the support of socially minded people, it has been decided to set up an altar in Lingyin Temple in Hangzhou from April 28th to hold a grand event. It is said that the purpose of holding this Kalachakra initiation is to eliminate domestic disasters and pray for world peace. In addition, in order to seek the blessing of the Buddha and benefit the masses, the event also plans to set up memorial and longevity tablets attached to the altar, inviting the Panchen Lama to provide assistance to the voluntary donations of believers; either to relieve the suffering of deceased relatives, or to pray for the blessings of living parents. From this point of view, building this event can be considered a measureless merit. However, many people have already come out to oppose this move, arguing that building the event is promoting superstition.

That's right, holding the City God Festival is a kind of superstition and should be prohibited. But isn't building the event also a kind of superstition, and should it be suppressed as well? However, our people's thoughts are always muddled and confused; on the one hand, we want to eradicate superstition, and on the other hand, we want to promote superstition. It seems as if eradicating superstition and promoting superstition, two absolutely contradictory things, can be carried out in parallel without contradicting each other, which is really ridiculous!

Some people say that the Kalachakra initiation and the City God Festival, although both are events, there is a big difference between them; that is, the former can save the country and relieve the world, while the latter will only waste money and harm the people. I think if the Buddha Dharma is boundless and can make the country peaceful and the world peaceful: even though the City God's abilities are small, doesn't he have the power to bring good fortune to a few pious men and women? As the saying goes, "Only the magistrate is allowed to set fires, but the common people are not allowed to light lamps," is this what it means?

Decadence and Recognition | I wish to encourage my fellow youths | 197

— Laopai

Why does our spirit become decadent? Generally speaking, it is due to physical weakness and congenital heredity. By extension, it is said that the vigor or decadence of the spirit is due to the strength or weakness of the body. For example, the physical strength of a person's body: a strong body has great physical strength, and a weak body has little physical strength. The same is true of the spirit: a strong body has a vigorous spirit, and a weak spirit is decadent. Further explaining the reasons for physical weakness, the first is due to illness, and the second is congenital heredity. The conclusion is that if you want the spirit not to be decadent, you can only strengthen the body first. With a strong body, the spirit will not be decadent.

In my opinion, physical strength or weakness does have an impact on the decadence of the spirit, but if we carefully examine the root causes of the phenomenon of decadence among our youth, I feel that the principle of "recognition" is a very important one. Many things are blind, wrong, and many unfortunate things that result from blindness and mistakes are mostly due to the fact that recognition is not thorough. Primitive humans worship nature, and medieval humans worship religion,: : : all because they do not recognize the true nature of these things. We know that recognition is based on deep and broad knowledge, keen vision, and sharp thinking to analyze and observe a thing. The clearer the analysis and the deeper the observation, the more one has exhausted the ability of recognition. Using recognition as a tool, we can uncover the coverings of all things and all phenomena, and only then can we approach the truth of things and phenomena.

We analyze the phenomenon of youth decadence and know that their decadence is not due to physical weakness, nor is it congenital heredity. We know that the problems that generally plague the minds of young people can be broadly divided into three points: the first is the problem of love, the second is the problem of career, and the third is the problem of thought. Among these three, the problem of thought is the most important. Having one of these three can make a certain youth decadent, and can make a living man become such a desolate and depressed person out of nowhere. To avoid this decadent fate, we must find its fundamental driving force in this current society. Because when we know this fundamental driving force, we will know how society produces this kind of magic. We know that modern society is a society full of contradictions and darkness, so that even if our young men and women have passion, they cannot find a lover, and even if they have a lover, they cannot be together, so that we sell ourselves cheaply, but still often suffer the misfortune of unemployment. As a result, we feel that this world is full of darkness, and we seem to have lost our guide, and we are involuntarily confused and shaken. In such a world, if we do not have a profound vision and recognize that although the present is full of contradictions, darkness, and evil, it is only the highest degree of development of an old social system, a inevitable phenomenon of the collapse, then we will easily be intimidated and suppressed by this dark side, and as a result, we will be discouraged and decadent. So in between, it is only a question of whether or not one recognizes it, there is definitely nothing else.

If we can truly and clearly understand the current society, then we can know that the sniper attacks on love and the uncompensated exploitation of intelligence and physical strength are all due to this unreasonable current social system. If we further examine history and know that this society is not fixed but is evolving, and know that when a social system develops to a certain stage, it cannot but collapse, then we can not only know the reasons for our pain, disappointment, and defeat, but we can also determine our own thoughts. In the face of the current clash between these two major trends | capitalism and socialism | we know which side we should tend towards, so as not to become a backward person without a way out or a future.

How can we achieve these things? It's all because of our recognition of reality! So I feel that the strength or weakness of the body is not enough to determine whether or not we are decadent. Conversely, recognizing or not recognizing is the fundamental reason for determining it. So I feel that if we want to completely lift the veil of the problem of decadence among our youth, we can only put more effort into "recognition."

Dying for Face 198

— Jianxiong

People are, after all, animals who die for face. Anything can be glossed over, but once face is at stake, they will not hesitate to sacrifice everything to win the honor of a face. It can be seen that in the eyes of the general public, it is regarded as a second life.

Face, this empty thing, cannot be touched or eaten, but it is given to so many people to be infatuated with and to strive for, until they die without being able to wake up. There must be a mysterious effect that exists.

On a small scale, the big men and gentlemen who usually have status and reputation in society have actually declared bankruptcy once they are attacked by a certain force. But they cannot live without Western-style houses, cannot live without cars, and their methods are still just as extravagant. In this way, someone will naturally lend them money, and the status, reputation, and life of the big men and gentlemen will be maintained.

Furthermore, a generation of modern ladies and young mistresses strive for face even more than big men and gentlemen. They would rather pawn their head and starve their stomachs, but they cannot live without buying overcoats and cannot live without wearing high-heeled leather shoes. Therefore, modern guys see them and cannot help but pursue them. If they cannot pursue them, they stuff them with banknotes. Finally, all the problems are solved. Because face is important, the scene can only be supported, and a hundred-spirit-like effect can be harvested. So the problem is expanded here.

When disputes arise between people, because of face, they refuse to give way to each other. As long as someone with face comes out to mediate, a word can calm things down. At the same time, if party A has more face than party B, party B has to submit and let party A handle things. Therefore, the loss of the three northeastern provinces is also due to the fact that China has no face in the international arena. So this face was occupied by the Japanese. The Chinese desperately fight for face for themselves, but they can "endure humiliation and bear heavy burdens" and throw away face to the foreigners, doing a favor for the Japanese. Perhaps fighting for face internally but not externally is a characteristic of the Chinese, and the problem is of course an exception!

There is still one point, which is also a manifestation of the Chinese "dying for face." When they lie straight in the coffin with their feet facing the sky, it is strange, it seems that the descendants know that their parents have the beautiful virtue of not forgetting face even in death, so they issue a large obituary, print it with a portrait, and ask celebrities to write things like "The wise man has withered" and "The invisible is safely admired." Finally, in the mourning notice, they bring out all the ancestors of the deceased who have face, such as "The late great-grandfather Mr. ×× was from ××, serving as an official to ××: : :" Then comes "The late father Mr. ×× was intelligent by nature and studied in Europe and America when he was young: : : served as the director of the ×× department: : :" It is nothing more than saying how loyal and honest the deceased was, how filial he was to his parents, and how much he loved the country. He had never done anything bad, whether it was Ah Mao or Ah Gou, it was always a thousand-piece set of stereotypical articles. It seems that if you don't boast like this, it is not enough to win a face for the deceased and win him posthumous glory (?). This is also such a comical and humorous thing! (The End)

His Beautiful Image Always Revolved in My Mind 199

Editor Sir,

I now have a perplexing problem that I have been unable to analyze for several years. I earnestly request that you, sir, would not hesitate to use your valuable space to provide me with a clear answer. Before I raise the issue, I must apologize to you, sir: I cannot reveal my name and address. I am well aware that this violates the rules of your column, but I have compelling reasons for doing so. Please forgive me and, as an exception, answer me this once!

I am a woman oppressed by a most stubborn family and am now twenty-four years old. When I was twenty, I worked for a certain company. At that time, a colleague introduced me to a boyfriend, who was three years older than me and very amiable. I was also very willing to be close to him. As time went on, we became even more intimate. Later, because I was extremely shy and could not bear the teasing of my colleagues, and because my stubborn parents monitored me with strict authority and regarded free love as shameful, I dared not reveal my love for him and could only swallow my voice and weep. After the Shanghai War broke out, I became unemployed and stayed at home, making it very difficult to be close to him. Although we sometimes met, we only exchanged a few words of casual conversation. Last spring, he became engaged to his female colleague. Of course, this matter seemed to have nothing to do with me, but in fact, the opposite was true. Whenever I sat quietly or rested, his beautiful image always revolved in my mind. Past events replayed themselves scene after scene without stopping. I repeatedly exhausted my spirit to try to eliminate these illusions and vexations, but I could never succeed. As a result, I was in great pain and felt like I was in a sick state all day long. I lost my parents' nurturing, and my only reliance is my brother. Although my situation is extremely difficult, no one cares about me. Recently, my mother has even said that I am old and eager to arrange a marriage for me. Such customs are inevitable. But unfortunately, I have been influenced by education and also because of him, which makes me feel very difficult. I think the reason why we need to get married is nothing more than to seek happiness and spiritual comfort. Now my mother believes in matchmakers and does not ask whether the other party is good or bad, only takes money as the goal. It can be asserted that my life's happiness and future are fraught with hidden crises. I have repeatedly advised her, but she is a stubborn person and will never listen. Furthermore, sometimes when I say something unpleasant to her, she faces me with tears in her eyes. I am most afraid of seeing others cry, let alone when I am in the position of a daughter. I cannot bear it, and after repeated consideration, the best solution is only to die. Moreover, living at home and relying on others for a living, I am often looked at with contempt. Relatives and friends often ridicule me. All kinds of difficulties are too numerous to mention. Being in this confused state makes my desire to die even stronger. Perhaps I am blinded by being in the situation, while outsiders can see clearly. Perhaps you, sir, can think of a way for me. Respectfully submitted by Anlan Fen.

Answer: This letter from Miss Lanfen reveals a gentle and docile personality in every line. However, precisely because she is too gentle, she cannot handle even simple problems. Therefore, what the editor wants to very solemnly tell Miss Lanfen is the eight words: "Be decisive in your actions and do not hesitate." As long as it is the right thing to do, go ahead and do it boldly. Otherwise, if you have too many concerns, you will achieve nothing. This is a very important point, and I hope you do not regard it as a cliché.

Your so-called "vexation" and so-called "various difficulties" can be summarized into two things: one is your lingering attachment to someone from the past, and the other is your unwillingness to let your mother arrange a marriage for you. Regarding the first point, the editor believes that it is entirely unnecessary. Humans are indeed emotional animals, and since you have very few social opportunities, it is natural to be reluctant to let go of a loved one, even though he may have forgotten you long ago. However, we must understand that life is not just about love, and our happiness is not solely encompassed by "love between men and women." If you fail in love, you can seek compensation in other areas. Conversely, even if you have a very happy love life, but there are many shortcomings in other aspects of life, it is not necessarily happiness. Therefore, the editor hopes that the first thing you do is to take love lightly. Furthermore, although you were very intimate, you did not dare to pursue him because you were shy, and he did not clearly express his love for you. In this situation, it is not really about love. Moreover, if he is still thinking about you now, it would be too foolish.

Men and women can create love by spending a long time together, but this does not mean that you can create love with just anyone you meet. This is like making friends. At first, you meet a stranger and feel a little unhappy with him, but later, after spending a long time together, you feel that he is not rigid, and you may even become friends. Therefore, the editor hopes that you will not have a very fearful attitude towards old-fashioned marriages. As long as you have a general understanding of the other person's character and appearance, and they are not very bad, then you can get married. It is not impossible to create love after marriage. In short, in our era, we should value the career we want to do more, and put love life in second place.

Coming back to the point, what the editor hopes for you and what I can offer you is only the word "decisiveness." Being afraid of embarrassment and worrying about everything is the worst thing. If you love someone, you can try your best to pursue them at the time and not be afraid of anything embarrassing. If it is not successful later, you should let it go quickly. Although you loved your former lover very much in your heart, the editor is afraid that he is still in the dark and does not know that you loved him so much! Perhaps if you had clearly expressed your love for him at the time, you and he might have already become a couple?
